Abstract: Understanding customer shopping trajectories is essential for enabling personalized shopping experiences. However, shopping records (i.e., customer's search, clicks, purchases, etc.) often span long time horizons over multiple years, resulting in extremely long trajectories that pose significant challenges for existing large language models (LLMs). Despite the importance of this problem, existing benchmarks are limited to short customer trajectories, while real-world trajectories from large e-commerce platforms are rarely accessible due to data privacy constraints. To address this gap, we introduce ShopTrajQA, a long-context evaluation benchmark constructed from real-world product information and simulated shopping trajectories. The dataset includes variants of up to 32k and 64k tokens, enabling systematic evaluation of model robustness under varying context lengths. Through comprehensive benchmarking of frontier LLMs, we identify critical performance gaps in reasoning over long shopping trajectory data. To address these challenges, we propose a Customer Agent Framework for ultra-long context management. Leveraging a Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) agentic training paradigm, our approach stores trajectories as external local files and trains the agent to autonomously retrieve and parse them through code-interpreter interactions (e.g., SQL queries), effectively bypassing the fixed in-context window constraints of LLMs. Experimental results demonstrate that our framework achieves strong performance for ShopTrajQA and shows generalization to other complex reasoning tasks.

### [94] [MC-PDD: Masked Corpus-Level Pretraining Data Detection for Black-Box Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07996)
*Kaixin Lan,Mu You,Tao Fang,Binkai Ou,Lidia S. Chao,Derek F. Wong*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预训练数据检测方法依赖模型概率分布，不适用于仅提供输入输出接口的闭源大模型，因此需要一种在黑盒环境下仍有效的检测方法。

Method: MC-PDD方法基于掩码语言建模思想，通过掩码文本中特定高信息量标记，利用模型预测缺失内容，并比较候选语料库与参考非成员语料库的预测命中率差异，进行统计显著性检验以判断是否曾被用于预训练。

Result: 实验表明，预训练数据与未见数据在预测命中率上存在明显且一致的差异，该方法在开源与闭源大模型上均表现良好，即使在更严格的黑盒设置下，性能也与现有方法相当。

Conclusion: MC-PDD是一种高效、实用的预训练数据检测方法，仅需标准API即可实现模型审计和数据版权验证，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Pretraining is fundamental to the development of Large Language Models (LLMs), yet the opacity of pretraining data complicates model analysis and raises ethical, legal, and fairness concerns. Detecting whether specific datasets were used during pretraining is, therefore, critical. Existing state-of-the-art methods typically rely on access to model probability distributions, making them unsuitable for closed-source LLMs that provide only input-output interfaces. To address this limitation, we introduce Masked Corpus-level Pretraining Data Detection (MC-PDD), a novel method inspired by the masked language modeling paradigm. MC-PDD masks highly specific tokens in each text and prompts the LLM to predict the missing content. It then assesses whether the difference in prediction hit rates between a candidate corpus and a reference non-member corpus is statistically significant. Based on this comparison, MC-PDD determines whether the candidate texts were likely included in the model's pretraining data. Experimental results demonstrate clear and consistent differences in prediction hit rates between pretrained and unseen data across three datasets, for both open-source and closed-source LLMs. Despite operating under a stricter black-box setting, MC-PDD achieves performance comparable to existing detection methods. Our approach enables practical applications such as model auditing and data copyright verification using only standard API access. Upon acceptance, we will publicly release the code and datasets.

### [95] [Summarization is Not Dead Yet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08000)
*Dongqi Liu,Chenxi Whitehouse,Zheng Zhao,Zhuchen Cao,Jian Li,Yabiao Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过多维度评估五个数据集和五种先进大语言模型，发现尽管大语言模型在流畅性和连贯性上表现更优，但在信息量、忠实度和事实准确性方面仍不及人类参考摘要，尤其在需要推理或综合的场景下。语言学分析还揭示了不同模型间风格趋同的现象。结论是：当前大语言模型虽提升了摘要质量的基线水平，但其上限仍低于人类能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型的发展，有观点认为其生成的摘要已可媲美甚至超越人类写作，这引发了对摘要是否仍是开放研究问题的质疑。本文旨在重新审视这一叙事，评估大语言模型在实际摘要任务中的真实表现。

Method: 采用多轨道评估方法，包括受控的人类评估、去偏的大语言模型作为裁判协议、基于外部知识的事实性验证以及语料级别的语言学分析，覆盖五个多样化数据集和五种前沿大语言模型。

Result: 人类参考摘要在信息量和忠实度方面仍具优势；大语言模型在表面连贯性和流畅性上更受青睐；事实性验证显示人类摘要在涉及推理或综合的陈述中更可靠；语言学分析发现不同模型输出存在风格同质化现象。

Conclusion: 当前大语言模型虽然提高了摘要质量的下限，但其性能上限仍低于人类水平，表明摘要任务依然是一个开放的研究问题。

Abstract: The progress of large language models (LLMs) has fueled claims that model-generated summaries rival or even surpass human-written references, raising questions about whether summarization remains an open research problem. We re-examine this narrative through a multi-track evaluation covering five diverse datasets and five state-of-the-art LLMs, combining controlled human assessment, bias-mitigated LLM-as-Judge protocols, factuality verification against external knowledge, and corpus-level linguistic analysis. Our findings reveal a more nuanced landscape in which human reference summaries continue to demonstrate advantages in informativeness and faithfulness, whereas LLM outputs are preferred mainly for surface-level coherence and fluency. Factuality verification indicates that human references remain more reliable, particularly for claims involving reasoning or synthesis, and linguistic analysis uncovers a pattern of stylistic homogeneity across different models. These observations suggest that current LLMs have raised the floor of summarization quality, but the ceiling of their performance remains below human capabilities.

Method: 提出RLSR（Reinforcement Learning for Source Rewriting）框架，利用下游翻译质量提升作为奖励信号，直接优化源文本重写模型，避免了对每种MT模型进行提示词调优。

### [98] [Diffusion Language Model Parallel Decoding via Product-of-Experts Bridge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08048)
*Juntong Shi,Brian L. Trippe,Jure Leskovec,Stefano Ermon,Minkai Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PoE-Bridge introduces an intermediate Product-of-Experts distribution to bridge the gap between diffusion language models (DLMs) and autoregressive (AR) models, enabling faster and more accurate text generation. It uses parallel drafting via DLM, rejection sampling to refine candidates toward the PoE, and importance sampling to align them with the AR target. Enhanced techniques like mixed-temperature sampling and elastic rejection windows improve diversity and efficiency. Empirically, PoE-Bridge achieves 5× speedup over standard DLM decoding and recovers 95%+ of AR model performance on challenging tasks.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To overcome the quality limitations of diffusion language models (DLMs) in text generation due to lack of token dependencies, while maintaining their speed advantage, by reducing the large distributional gap between DLMs and autoregressive (AR) models that hinders efficient importance sampling.

Method: Proposes PoE-Bridge: constructs a Product-of-Experts (PoE) distribution from DLM proposal and AR target; uses DLM to draft multiple continuations in parallel; applies rejection sampling to move candidates toward PoE; then uses importance sampling to correct candidates toward AR target. Includes mixed-temperature sampling and elastic rejection windows for better diversity and efficiency.

Result: PoE-Bridge achieves 5× faster decoding than standard DLM methods and recovers at least 95% of the performance of the target AR model, significantly narrowing the quality gap on complex tasks like mathematical reasoning and code generation.

Conclusion: PoE-Bridge effectively bridges the distributional gap between DLMs and AR models through an intermediate PoE distribution, enabling high-speed, high-quality text generation. It offers a practical and scalable solution for leveraging the strengths of both paradigms.

Abstract: Diffusion language models (DLMs) offer substantial speed advantages through parallel decoding, but the lack of token dependencies limits generation quality compared to autoregressive (AR) models. Recent progress attempts to bridge the gap via importance sampling, with DLM being the proposal and AR being the target. However, due to the huge gap between their distributions, the sampling requires a large number of particles and is thus expensive to compute. In this paper, we introduce PoE-Bridge, a novel decoding framework that drastically improves generation speed and accuracy by introducing an intermediate distribution to bridge the gap. The distribution is constructed as a Product-of-Experts (PoE) of the DLM proposal and the AR target. With the intermediate distribution, we first use the DLM to draft multiple continuations in parallel, then apply rejection sampling to verify the drafted tokens and move the resulting candidates toward the PoE. We then use importance sampling to further correct the PoE-aligned candidates toward the AR target. We further propose several improved techniques, including mixed-temperature sampling for enhanced diversity and elastic rejection windows for reducing wasted verification. Empirically, PoE-Bridge achieves significantly improved accuracy with $5\times$ speedup over the standard DLM decoding approach, and recovers at least 95% of the target AR model's performance, efficiently advancing most of the quality gap on challenging mathematical reasoning and coding tasks. Our code is available at https://github.com/juntongshi48/poe-bridge.

We introduce a framework for training and evaluating indexing experts, establishing a baseline for index-aware sign language modeling. ### [101] ["I understand your perspective": LLM Persuasion and Sycophancy through the Lens of Communicative Action Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08076)

Method: 使用来自persuasive subreddit ChangeMyView的真实对话数据，模拟人类与大语言模型之间的辩论；通过对比成功改变原发帖者观点的人类与模型生成的反驳意见，分析其中言语意图的分布；并进行众包评估以判断人们对不同来源反驳意见的偏好。

This work explores the persuasive potential of LLMs through the framework of Jürgen Habermas' Theory of Communicative Action. It examines whether LLMs express illocutionary intent (i.e., pragmatic functions of language such as conveying knowledge, building trust, or signaling similarity) in ways that are comparable to human communication. We simulate online discussions between opinion holders and LLMs using conversations from the persuasive subreddit ChangeMyView. We then compare the likelihood of illocutionary intents in human-written and LLM-generated counter-arguments, specifically those that successfully changed the original poster's view. Finally, crowd-sourced workers find LLM-generated counter-arguments more agreeable and consistently prefer them over human-written ones. On the contrary, training LLMs with human preferences effectively tunes them to mirror human communication patterns, particularly nuanced communicative actions, potentially increasing individuals' susceptibility to their influence.

### [102] [Support Vector Rubrics: Closing the Gap Between Self-Generated and Human Rubrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08077)
*Mengyuan Sun,Yu Li,Zhuohao Yu,Shikun Zhang,Wei Ye*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SVR (Support Vector Rubrics) addresses the discriminative gap in LLM evaluation by reframing rubric construction as max-margin boundary learning. It uses preference data to mine contrastive features, learns a prompt-conditioned selector and global rubric weights, and iteratively refines rubrics via support-pair selection and adversarial probing. On RubricBench, SVR reduces the gap with human rubrics from 24.1 to 0.3 points and outperforms baselines; it also transfers across judges and performs competitively on RewardBench and RM-Bench.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Self-generated rubrics often fail to discriminate between similar responses, leading to a performance gap compared to human-annotated rubrics. The core issue is an objective mismatch: self-rubrics describe good responses but don’t effectively distinguish close candidates.

Method: SVR recasts rubric construction as max-margin boundary learning. It builds a rubric bank from contrastive features in preference pairs, jointly learns a prompt-conditioned selector and global rubric weights, and iteratively improves the bank through support-pair selection and adversarial probing of hard negatives.

Result: On RubricBench, SVR reduces the gap to human reference rubrics from 24.1 to 0.3 points, outperforms strong self-rubric and judge baselines, and transfers across judges without retraining. On RewardBench 1&2 and RM-Bench, it remains competitive with dedicated reward models, showing strong generalization and reward modeling capability.

Conclusion: Boundary-defining rubrics, learned through SVR, provide a principled solution to closing the discriminative gap in LLM evaluation, enabling more accurate and transferable assessment of model outputs.

Abstract: Rubric-based evaluation is a promising paradigm for judging large language model (LLM) outputs, yet self-generated rubrics lag human-annotated criteria on hard instances. We argue this discriminative gap reflects an objective mismatch: self-generated rubrics describe good responses, whereas effective criteria must discriminate between close candidates. To close this gap, we introduce SVR (Support Vector Rubrics), a framework that recasts rubric construction as max-margin boundary learning over preference data. SVR mines contrastive features from preference pairs into a rubric bank, learns a prompt-conditioned selector together with global rubric weights, and iteratively refines the bank through support-pair selection and adversarial probing of hard negatives. At inference, given only the prompt, SVR retrieves the top-rubrics from the bank and scores responses. On RubricBench, SVR narrows the gap to human reference rubrics from 24.1 to 0.3 points and outperforms strong self-rubric and judge baselines, and the learned bank transfers across judges without retraining. On RewardBench 1&2, and RM-Bench, it remains competitive with dedicated reward models, demonstrating broader reward modeling capability. Overall, boundary-defining rubrics offer a principled route to closing the discriminative gap in LLM evaluation.

### [103] [Aligned but Not Partner-Specific: Distinguishing How Multimodal LLM Agents Succeed in Reference Games Without Human-Like Conventions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08081)
*Po-Ya Angela Wang,Chinmaya Mishra,Aslı Özyürek,Paula Rubio-Fernández,Esam Ghaleb*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过比较人类与多模态代理在重复参照游戏中的表现，探讨了大型多模态模型（MLLMs）是否真正形成了基于互动历史的特定于伙伴的指称惯例。研究提出一种受控的伪双人组基线方法，打破伙伴历史以检验标签对齐是否依赖于特定互动。结果发现，人类在对话中通过协同适应压缩描述、提升标签一致性；而代理则保持固定高耗能描述，标签重叠度高但不随互动变化，表明其协调是通过冗长描述而非形成紧凑的历史依赖表达实现的，缺乏真正的惯例形成能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明，多模态大模型虽能对齐标签，但无法在多轮交互中提高效率，即未能形成简洁、基于共享历史的指称惯例。关键问题是：这种标签对齐是否反映了真实的伙伴特定接地，还是仅表现为对任务词汇的共同使用？需要一种方法来区分这两种机制。

Method: 采用来自KTH Tangrams语料库的人类双人组数据作为基准，构建与真实双人组结构一致但破坏伙伴历史的‘伪双人组’基线。通过三个分析层次（任务能力、描述策略、对齐动态）对比人类与多模态代理的表现，评估标签对齐是否依赖真实互动历史。

Result: 人类表现出显著的协作适应：描述逐渐缩短，标签对齐程度随互动增加而上升，体现为高效交流。相比之下，多模态代理从第一轮起即保持冗长描述，标签重叠度始终接近上限，且在真实与伪双人组间无统计差异，说明其对齐并非源于互动历史。

Conclusion: 多模态大模型虽然能实现标签对齐，但并未形成真正意义上的伙伴特定惯例。它们通过冗长描述达成协调，而非发展出历史依赖、简洁高效的指称表达，这表明其沟通机制与人类自然对话存在本质差异。

Abstract: Repeated reference games test whether interlocutors replace their initially long descriptions with shorter, partner-specific conventions grounded in shared interaction history. Prior work shows that multimodal LLMs fail to become more efficient across rounds, although they align on the labels they use. How can we determine whether this alignment reflects partner-specific grounding rather than a shared task vocabulary? We address this question by comparing capable multimodal agent dyads with human dyads from the KTH Tangrams corpus. Our novel methodological contribution is a constrained pseudo-dyad baseline that matches the original referential task structure, but breaks partner history. This baseline enables us to test whether the observed label alignment depends on interaction with a specific partner. Across three analytic layers (task competence, description strategy, alignment dynamics), we find clear differences. Humans reduce effort through entrainment, compressing descriptions and increasing label alignment with partners. Agents instead maintain fixed effort levels, producing verbose descriptions from round one, with near-ceiling label overlap that is statistically indistinguishable between real and pseudo dyads. MLLMs thus achieve coordination without convention, succeeding by verbose description rather than by forming the compact, history-dependent referring expressions characteristic of human dialogue.

*Xiyan Fu,Wei Lu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为SEMJ的自演化多语言裁判模型，利用跨语言不一致性作为互补评估信号，而非将其视为噪声。通过构建多语言输入变体、收集独立判断与推理过程，并将不一致结果反馈用于自我反思与重评，实现了迭代优化。实验表明，SEMJ在准确性和跨语言一致性上均优于投票和反思基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将多语言不一致性视为噪声并采用投票或聚合来缓解，但本文发现这种不一致性实际上能提供互补的评估信息，从而提升评价性能上限。

Method: 提出SEMJ模型，通过生成多语言输入变体，收集各语言独立的判断与理由，并将不一致结果反馈用于自我反思和重新评估，实现迭代优化。

Result: 在多个基准测试中，SEMJ在准确性和跨语言一致性方面均显著优于投票和反思类基线方法；分析显示不一致性有效触发了高质量的重新评估。

Conclusion: 跨语言不一致性并非缺陷，而是可被利用的有益信号。SEMJ通过主动挖掘该信号，实现了更优的多语言评估性能。

Abstract: Multilingual LLM-as-a-judge is widely used to evaluate model outputs across languages, but suffers from cross-lingual inconsistency (Fu and Liu, 2025). Existing methods typically treat this inconsistency as noise and mitigate it through voting or aggregation. In this work, we instead show that multilingual inconsistency can provide complementary evaluation signals. Our oracle analysis finds that sampling judgments across languages yields a higher performance upper bound than single-language judging, indicating that different languages potentially include complementary judgments. Motivated by this finding, we propose SEMJ, a self-evolving multilingual judge that leverages cross-lingual inconsistency for iterative refinement. SEMJ constructs multilingual variants of each input, collects independent judgments and rationales, and feeds inconsistent outputs back for self-reflection and re-evaluation. Experiments on multiple benchmarks show that SEMJ consistently outperforms voting and reflection baselines in both accuracy and cross-lingual consistency. Further analysis shows that inconsistency triggers useful re-evaluation, which improves judgment quality.

</details>


### [105] [Cross Paraphrastic Invariance Learning for Hallucination Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08157)
*Shanshan Lin,Dongsheng Hong,Sibo Ju,Chao Chen,Sihong Xie,Xiangwen Liao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CPIL是一种两阶段西米斯框架，通过生成文档-主张对的改写视图作为正例，并挖掘同文档、异标签对作为难负例，以实现对表面形式的不变性对齐和敏感决策边界的增强。该方法在仅使用约1%标注数据的情况下，在LLM-AggreFact基准上超越了强基线模型的F1分数，表现出卓越的预测性能和标签效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖昂贵的LLM评估管道或大量人工标注，导致成本高且难以扩展。因此需要一种高效利用有限标注数据的方法来减少幻觉并提升生成内容的可信度。

Method: CPIL采用两阶段训练：第一阶段通过对比学习构建一个对改写不变且具备上下文感知能力的嵌入空间；第二阶段添加轻量级分类器进行二元有根据性判断。具体包括生成改写视图作为正样本，以及挖掘同文档反标签样本作为难负样本。

Result: 在包含11个任务的LLM-AggreFact基准测试中，CPIL在仅使用约1%标注数据的情况下，显著优于多个强基线模型的F1得分，证明其在预测性能与标签效率上的优势。

Conclusion: CPIL通过跨改写不变性学习有效提升了大语言模型生成内容的可信度，同时大幅降低对标注数据的依赖，为低成本、高效率的事实核查提供了新范式。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) frequently generate hallucinations, which are unsupported by a source document. To avoid costly LLM-as-evaluator pipelines and the heavy annotation demands of existing classifiers, we propose CPIL (Cross Paraphrastic Invariance Learning), a two-stage Siamese framework that maximizes the utility of existing labeled data. Concretely, CPIL constructs informative training pairs by: (i) generating paraphrastic views of each document-claim example as positives, and explicitly aligning their representations to enforce invariance to surface form; and (ii) mining same-document, opposite-label pairs as hard negatives to sharpen document-sensitive decision boundaries. Then CPIL conduct a two-stage model training: Stage 1 performs contrastive pretraining to learn a paraphrase-invariant, grounding-aware embedding space; and Stage 2 attaches a lightweight classifier for binary groundedness. On the LLM-AggreFact benchmark (11 tasks), CPIL surpasses strong baselines concerning F1 scores with only ~1% labeled data, showing its prediction superiority and label efficiency.

</details>

### [106] [Offline Reinforcement Learning for Plasma Control in Nuclear Fusion: Codebase and Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07550)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于DIII-D托卡马克的历史放电数据构建动态模型，建立闭环评估环境，涵盖四个全剖面跟踪任务；采用统一协议评估多种模仿学习和离线强化学习基线方法。

Result: 基于模型的离线强化学习方法在大多数目标上表现最优，但无单一方法在所有任务上占优，表明动力学建模在复杂长时序控制中至关重要。

Conclusion: RL4F为核聚变等离子体控制提供了首个标准化离线强化学习基准，推动该领域算法发展，并促进跨领域的离线强化学习研究。

Abstract: Offline reinforcement learning (RL) offers a promising route for developing plasma controllers from historical tokamak data, since online trial-and-error on real devices is costly and risky. However, progress in this direction remains difficult to measure due to the lack of a standardized offline RL benchmark for realistic multi-actuator, long-horizon plasma control problems in nuclear fusion. We introduce RL4F, an Offline Reinforcement Learning Benchmark for Plasma Control in Nuclear Fusion, providing closed-loop evaluation environments and baseline comparisons across four full-profile tracking tasks: rotation, density, temperature, and pressure. The dynamics function underlying the evaluation environment is built from historical discharge data from DIII-D, a real-world Tokamak. We evaluate a broad set of imitation learning and offline RL baselines under a unified protocol. We find that offline model-based RL methods obtain the best average performance on most objectives, although no single method dominates all tasks, highlighting the importance of dynamics modeling in complex, long-horizon plasma control tasks. To foster further research, we open-source the codebase, datasets, and evaluation framework, providing a benchmark not only for the fusion community but also for algorithm development in offline RL.

The Medical Recommender System (MedicalRec) is a transformer-based model used for item recommendations in this study. ### [108] [SPIN: Decentralized Swarm Control via Tensorized Policy Coordination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07557)
*Zhaowen Fan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为SPIN的框架，用于在资源受限的边缘平台上实现去中心化的多智能体集群协调。通过将集群拓扑建模为压缩张量网络，并使用矩阵乘积态（MPS）链分解联合策略张量，将计算复杂度从指数级 $O(n^m)$ 降低至线性 $O(m \cdot n \cdot χ^2)$，从而克服了动作空间膨胀和通信延迟问题。引入一种解耦的混合神经符号控制流程：离线预训练的多层神经网络作为结构协调编码器，将几何特征映射为环境目标度量；运行时则通过直接应用Radon-Nikodým导数作为零样本重要性重加权滤波器，实现即时行为调整。在多种任务场景下验证了该框架的有效性，包括跟踪、分散覆盖及多目标协同，表现出稳定的目标导向运动、抗塌陷的空间扩散以及结构化子群形成能力，为低功耗边缘集群智能提供了数学上可解释且可扩展的解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前去中心化多智能体系统在资源受限的边缘平台上的协调面临两大核心挑战：一是联合动作空间随智能体数量呈指数级增长，导致计算不可行；二是高延迟通信开销限制了实时响应能力。现有方法难以在保证性能的同时满足低功耗与实时性的要求，亟需一种新型架构来突破这些瓶颈。

Method: 提出基于张量网络的SPIN框架，将集群拓扑表示为压缩张量结构；采用矩阵乘积态（MPS）对局部多智能体团块的联合策略张量进行因子分解，实现计算复杂度从指数级到线性的转变；设计一种解耦的混合神经符号控制管道：前段使用离线预训练的多层神经网络将手工几何特征映射为抽象环境目标度量；运行时利用Radon-Nikodým导数作为零样本重要性重加权机制，实现无需在线训练的即时行为适应。

Result: 在多个仿真任务中（如目标跟踪、分散覆盖、多目标协作），系统展现出稳定的定向运动、抗塌陷的空间分布特性以及结构化的子群形成能力。计算效率显著提升，符合低功耗边缘部署需求，验证了该框架在复杂环境下实现高效、鲁棒、可扩展的去中心化智能的可行性。

Conclusion: SPIN框架通过张量网络与神经符号系统的结合，为资源受限边缘平台上的大规模多智能体协同提供了一条数学严谨、计算高效且可落地的技术路径，是迈向低功耗、高可靠边缘集群智能的重要一步。

Abstract: Decentralized multi-agent swarm coordination on resource-constrained edge platforms remains fundamentally bottlenecked by the exponential scaling of joint action spaces and high-latency communication overhead. This paper introduces the Swarm Policy Interference Network (SPIN) framework, an architectural paradigm that bypasses these limitations by modeling swarm topologies as a compressed tensor network. We factorize the joint policy tensors of local multi-agent cliques into Matrix Product State (MPS) chains, reducing the computational complexity of evaluation from an exponential $O(n^m)$ wall to a strictly linear $O(m \cdot n \cdot χ^2)$ constraint. To bridge local continuous spatial geometry with this discrete algebraic backend without requiring power-intensive online training loops, we introduce a decoupled, hybrid neuro-symbolic control pipeline. Local multi-layered neural networks operate as structural coordination encoders, pre-trained offline to nonlinearly map hand-engineered geometric descriptors into abstract environmental target measures. At runtime, edge agents execute instantaneous behavioral adaptations by applying the Radon-Nikodým derivative directly as a zero-shot importance-reweighting filter. We validate the framework within a discrete-time multi-agent simulation sandbox spanning tracking, decentralized dispersion/area coverage, and multi-goal coordination regimes. Qualitative telemetry demonstrates that the integrated pipeline achieves stable target-directed motion, anti-collapse spatial spreading under decentralized constraints, and structured subgroup formation across multiple targets, providing a mathematically grounded route to tractable, low-power edge swarm intelligence.

</details>


### [109] [Boundary Variance Inflation Causes Acquisition Bias in Gaussian Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07561)
*Maria Bånkestad,Sanna Jarl,Jens Sjölund*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 高斯过程在有界域上使用平稳核时，边界附近后验方差被夸大，导致贝叶斯优化中的过度探索。本文揭示了这一现象的根本原因在于核相关邻域在边界处被截断，形成与观测无关的几何畸变，且随维度增加而加剧。该畸变导致不同类型的采集函数表现出不同的选择模式：方差最大化倾向于选择角落，负集成后验方差和期望预测信息增益则倾向于选择轴对齐的内部壳层。这些行为完全由核几何决定，而非目标函数，可能主导实际优化过程。为此，作者提出一种无需依赖具体函数的选择特征诊断工具，适用于任意采集函数、核函数及有界域几何。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决高斯过程在有界域上因边界截断导致的后验方差膨胀问题，揭示其对贝叶斯优化中采集策略的负面影响，特别是采集行为被核几何主导而非任务需求的现象。

Method: 通过分析核相关邻域在边界处的几何截断机制，识别出观察无关的畸变来源；利用理论推导和数值实验分析三类典型采集函数的行为模式；提出一种函数无关的选择特征诊断方法，用于量化不同设置下的采集偏差。

Result: 证实边界截断引发的几何畸变是导致采集偏差的根本原因；发现不同采集函数在有界域中呈现特定的空间选择偏好（如角落或内部壳层）；提出的诊断工具可有效量化各类采集策略的边界偏差程度。

Conclusion: 边界引起的采集偏差源于核几何的内在特性，而非目标函数本身。该偏差可能显著影响贝叶斯优化性能，建议在设计采集策略时考虑域几何与核结构的匹配性，并推荐使用所提出的诊断工具评估和缓解此类问题。

Abstract: Gaussian processes with stationary kernels on bounded domains exhibit inflated posterior variance near the boundary. Despite being a long-recognized artifact in geostatistics and a source of over-exploration in Bayesian optimization, the causes and effects of boundary-induced acquisition bias are underexplored. We trace the root cause to a simple geometric mechanism: the truncation of the kernel correlation neighborhood at the domain boundary creates an observation-independent distortion that worsens with dimensionality. We show how this distortion manifests across three acquisition classes: variance maximization concentrates selections at the corners, whereas negative integrated posterior variance and expected predictive information gain move selections inward to axis-aligned interior shells. These patterns arise without reference to any objective function, meaning that acquisition behavior can be dominated by kernel geometry rather than the desired task-specific uncertainty. To quantify this, we introduce a function-free selection-profile diagnostic for arbitrary acquisitions, kernels, and bounded-domain geometries.

</details>


### [110] [Emergence via Phase Transitions: Mechanism Landscapes and Universal Convergence Across Complex Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07563)
*Truong Xuan Khanh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出层次涌现框架（HEF），用以解释机器学习、生物学和物理学中独立演化系统趋向相似宏观结构的现象。该框架将涌现视为受热力学与信息理论定律约束的机制景观中的相变，存在一个临界能量阈值Ec，区分探索与收敛两种状态。在结构假设下，证明了物理可行性，推导出严格度量收缩，并建立对初始条件无关的唯一固定点表示的收敛性。通过有效信息和机制竞争熵连接因果涌现。实验验证了模块化算术Transformer中的延迟泛化（“grokking”）现象：92%的实验显示权重范数在grokking前出现峰值；归一化准确率曲线收敛至tanh拐点（R²=0.93），所有模型最终性能趋同于0.9745±0.014，不受初始化、权重衰减或训练比例影响。HEF作为可证伪的数学框架，为复杂系统中的收敛现象提供研究基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 跨领域系统（如机器学习、生物、物理）虽微观细节不同，却常呈现高度相似的宏观结构，亟需统一框架解释此类涌现收敛现象。现有理论难以涵盖多系统共性，需构建一个基于物理与信息原理的可验证数学模型。

Method: 提出层级涌现框架（HEF），将涌现建模为机制景观中的相变，引入临界能量阈值Ec，划分探索与收敛阶段；结合热力学与信息论约束，通过结构假设证明物理可行性、度量收缩及唯一固定点收敛；利用有效信息与机制竞争熵关联因果涌现；通过大规模实验（111次）分析Transformer中的grokking现象，检验框架预测。

Result: 实验发现权重范数在grokking前92%的运行中出现峰值；归一化准确率曲线高度一致地符合tanh型拐点（R²=0.93），体现Landau-Ginzburg类普适性；所有模型收敛至0.9745±0.014的性能水平，不受初始条件、正则化或训练程度影响。结果支持HEF的预测能力。

Conclusion: HEF并非万能理论，而是一个可证伪的数学框架，为跨领域复杂系统中的收敛现象提供统一建模与分析工具，具有广泛的适用潜力与实证支撑。

Abstract: Across machine learning, biology, and physics, independently evolving systems often converge toward strikingly similar high-level structures despite radically different microscopic details. Grokking circuits converge across random seeds, evolutionary lineages rediscover similar metabolic solutions, and renormalization flows approach common fixed points. We propose the Hierarchical Emergence Framework (HEF) as a candidate universality framework for such convergence phenomena. HEF models emergence as a phase transition in a mechanism landscape constrained by thermodynamic and information-theoretic laws. The framework introduces a critical energy threshold Ec separating an exploration regime with competing mechanisms from a convergence regime governed by a unique minimum-cost mechanism. Under structural assumptions, we prove physical feasibility, derive strict metric contraction, and establish convergence toward a unique fixed-point representation independent of initial conditions. We further connect this convergence structure to causal emergence through Effective Information and mechanism competition entropy. To test the framework, we study delayed generalization ("grokking") in modular arithmetic transformers across 111 experiments. We identify a reproducible empirical fingerprint of the Ec transition: the weight norm peaks systematically before grokking in 92% of runs. Normalized accuracy curves collapse onto a tanh kink (R^2=0.93) consistent with a Landau-Ginzburg universality class, and all grokked models converge to 0.9745+/-0.014 regardless of initialization, weight decay, or training fraction (ANOVA p>0.13). HEF is not presented as a universal theory of emergence, but as a falsifiable mathematical scaffold for studying convergence phenomena across complex systems.

</details>


### [111] [STARIXNet: Multivariate and Multi-attribute Deep Learning Approach to Real-Time Resource Allocation in Cloud Platforms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07565)
*Ahmed Abdulaal,Maruf Aytekin,Thilaga kumaran Srinivasan,Tomer Lancewicki*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: STARIXNet 是一种轻量级神经网络，用于在多变量空间中智能扩展云平台上的微服务，通过捕捉多个系统指标之间的时空关系来优化资源分配。它结合了季节性、时间序列、自回归整合和外生模式（STARIX），并采用聚合策略以优先保证服务稳定性与成本效益，而非单纯追求预测精度。在沃尔玛的实际部署中，该方法实现了10%至50%的成本节约，并提升了服务稳定性和用户体验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前微服务扩展方案多局限于单一指标（如仅CPU使用率），且将问题视为纯预测任务，忽视低估风险和响应延迟，同时现有方法计算复杂，难以在大规模实时场景中应用。因此需要一种更高效、更稳定的多变量扩展机制。

Method: 提出STARIXNet模型，融合季节性（S）、时间性（T）、自回归整合（AR）与外生因素（X）的多维特征，建模多个相关系统指标间的时空依赖关系，设计聚合策略以生成最终的扩缩容决策，兼顾服务稳定性与成本效率。

Result: 在真实生产环境中部署于沃尔玛关键微服务，实现10%至50%的成本节省；显著提升系统稳定性与客户体验，优于现有方法。

Conclusion: STARIXNet通过多变量时空建模与合理的决策聚合机制，在保证服务稳定性的前提下有效降低资源开销，适用于大规模、实时的微服务扩展场景。

Abstract: Intelligent scaling of microservices in cloud platforms is crucial for mitigating escalating compute costs while avoiding service disruptions. Current solutions are limited to the univariate space, typically focusing on CPU usage alone to drive scaling decisions. Moreover, they address the problem as a purely forecasting task, focusing on prediction precision while neglecting the greater risks of underestimation and delays in system responsiveness. Alternative solutions are computationally complex, making them impractical for large-scale, real-time deployments. To address these challenges, we present STARIXNet, a lightweight neural network that guides resource allocation decisions in the multivariate space by capturing spatio-temporal relationships among multiple system metrics. STARIXNet models multiple quasi-dependent attributes, in particular the (S)easonal, (T)emporal, (A)uto-(R)egressive (I)ntegrated, and e(X)ogenous patterns, then implements an aggregation policy to finalize scaling decisions, prioritizing service stability, followed by cost-efficiency, over raw forecast accuracy. We empirically demonstrate the performance of STARIXNet by benchmarking against existing solutions in real-world settings. STARIXNet is deployed for critical production microservices at Walmart achieving tangible savings ranging from 10\% to 50\%, in addition to intangible benefits through improved service stability and customer experience.

</details>


### [112] [TriHead-GAN: A Generative Adversarial Network with Triple-Head Discriminator for Carbon Emission Time Series Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07569)
*Zesen Wang,Lijuan Lan,Yonggang Li,Chunhua Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出TriHead-GAN框架，通过三头判别器联合监督碳排放数据的分布真实性、变量间依赖关系和时序步进平滑性，结合自注意力与局部卷积的生成器及抗平滑损失，有效生成具有真实波动特性的高频率城市碳排放时间序列，显著提升低资源场景下的下游预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型在碳排放数据建模中缺乏对变量间相关性和时序阶差统计特性的有效监督，导致生成序列过于平滑且不具现实波动性，限制了深度学习模型在城市级高频率碳排放监测中的应用。

Method: 提出基于Transformer的对抗生成框架TriHead-GAN，其三头判别器分别负责：Wasserstein分布真实性评估、无泄漏回归捕捉跨变量依赖、相邻差分预测保证时序步进平滑性；生成器采用全局自注意力与局部卷积结合结构，引入每步噪声注入和抗平滑损失以匹配一阶差分统计特征。

Result: 在自收集的长沙碳排放数据集、中国与美国两个公开数据集以及ETTh1基准上，TriHead-GAN在多数设置下优于主流基线方法，生成的合成时间窗口显著提升了低资源碳监测场景下的下游预测精度。

Conclusion: TriHead-GAN通过多维度监督机制有效生成具备真实动态特征的碳排放时间序列，为城市级高频率碳排放监测提供了可靠数据支持，推动了气候政策与碳边境调节机制的数据基础建设。

Abstract: Accurate carbon emission monitoring is critical for climate policy and emerging regulatory mechanisms such as the EU Carbon Border Adjustment Mechanism, yet city-level high-frequency monitoring data remain extremely scarce, severely limiting data-hungry deep learning models. Time series generation is a natural remedy, but existing GAN and diffusion-based generators often provide limited explicit supervision for the domain structure of carbon emission data: they may match marginal distributional statistics while insufficiently preserving cross-variable correlations between CO$_2$ and co-emitted pollutants and meteorological factors, and tend to collapse the first-difference statistics of atmospheric measurements, producing sequences that are smooth on average but lack the realistic step-wise variability of the underlying signals. We propose TriHead-GAN, a Transformer-based adversarial framework whose triple-head discriminator jointly supervises three complementary aspects of the joint distribution: distributional authenticity via a Wasserstein critic, cross-variable dependency via leakage-free regression of the target variable, and step-wise temporal smoothness via adjacent-difference prediction. The generator combines global self-attention with local temporal convolution, per-step noise injection, and an anti-smoothing loss that matches first-difference statistics. Experiments on the self-collected Changsha Carbon dataset, two public carbon datasets (China, US), and the ETTh1 benchmark show that TriHead-GAN achieves favorable performance over mainstream baselines on the vast majority of settings, and that the resulting synthetic windows improve downstream forecasting accuracy in low-resource carbon monitoring scenarios.

### [113] [Enabling KV Caching of Shared Prefix for Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07571)
*Younghun Go,Jaehoon Han,Changyong Shin,Chuk Yoo,Gyeongsik Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为bicache的新方法，用于解决扩散语言模型（DLMs）中共享前缀的键值（KV）缓存问题。传统基于LLM的缓存技术在DLMs中因双向注意力机制导致上下文动态变化而失效，造成精度崩溃。bicache通过分析发现浅层中的共享前缀KV具有稳定性，可安全复用，并动态确定可复用的安全层数，从而避免冗余计算。实验表明，与现有方法相比，bicache在不引起精度下降的情况下，将服务吞吐量提升了36.3%至98.3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KV缓存技术假设一旦计算完成，键值对（KVs）保持不变，但在扩散语言模型（DLMs）中，由于双向注意力机制，任意令牌的更新都会影响整个上下文及其对应的KVs，导致共享前缀的KVs被破坏，进而引发模型精度严重下降。因此需要一种专为DLMs设计的新缓存机制。

Method: 提出bicache方法，基于对共享前缀在不同层中稳定性的分析，动态识别可用于复用的浅层安全深度，仅在这些层复用共享前缀的KVs，其余深层则重新计算以保证准确性。该方法有效减少冗余计算，同时维持高精度。

Result: 实验结果显示，与现有技术相比，bicache在保持模型精度几乎不变（仅0-1.8%差异）的前提下，显著提升服务吞吐量36.3%至98.3%。

Conclusion: bicache是首个适用于扩散语言模型中共享前缀的键值缓存技术，解决了双向注意力带来的缓存一致性问题，实现了高吞吐、高准确率的DLM服务，为高效推理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Key-value (KV) caching for shared prefixes is essential for high-throughput large language model (LLM) serving, but it faces critical challenges in emerging diffusion language models (DLMs). In DLMs, bidirectional attention means that updating any token dynamically alters the entire context and its corresponding KVs. Thus, existing caching techniques developed for LLMs, which assume that KVs remain invariant once computed, corrupt the shared prefix KVs. Our experiments show that applying these techniques to DLMs causes model accuracy to collapse to near zero.
  To unlock high-throughput DLM serving, we propose bidirectional prefix caching, bicache, the first KV caching technique for shared prefixes in DLMs. bicache is designed based on key observations from our comprehensive analysis: shared prefix KVs remain stable and reusable in shallow layers, while the depth of shallow layers depends on the fraction of shared prefix tokens in each request. Thus, bicache dynamically identifies a safe layer depth for reusing shared prefix KVs and eliminates redundant computation. Evaluations demonstrate that bicache significantly improves serving throughput by 36.3%-98.3% compared to existing techniques without accuracy collapse (only 0-1.8% difference).

</details>


### [114] [When Should an AI Scientist Stop? Verifiable Experiment Steering and Refusal for Autonomous Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07576)
*Neel Tushar Shah,Manglam Kartik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CARTOGRAPH 是一个面向人工智能科学家的验证层，结合了未解空间实验引导（select）、显式模糊性闭合（resolve）和基于残差的库不充分性检测（refuse）。在局部线性高斯桥框架下，原始未解投影为各向同性的未解费舍尔信息迹，而 CARTOGRAPH-A 是精确的未解 A-最优规则；局部比较器如 EIG 和 Box-Hill 并非全局等价物。在五个测试平台上，CARTOGRAPH-A 在 d=8 时以 129W/0T/15L 的战绩显著优于原始投影（p < 10^-21），且在结构化级联中可识别并撤销三个超出库外的药代动力学机制，同时保持一个受扰动的库内对照被持续识别。低维药代动力学与过滤后的 EPA 设置中，理论预测的近似平局与实际观察一致。对 40 个已发表 A-Lab 自主材料系统中的阳性声明进行回溯审计，拒绝机制成功标记所有 4 个后来被手动重新分析判定为不确定的声明，同时通过了 32/36 个确认有效的声明。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 AI 科学系统缺乏对模型不确定性、库外机制识别及不可靠预测的可靠验证机制，导致错误结论可能被误认为有效。本文旨在构建一个可解释、可验证的验证层，提升 AI 科学系统的可信度与安全性。

Method: 提出 CARTOGRAPH 框架，包含 select（实验引导）、resolve（模糊性闭合）、refuse（拒绝异常预测）三模块。基于局部线性高斯桥建模未解空间，利用 A-最优准则优化选择策略，通过残差分析检测库外机制，并引入 EIG 与 Box-Hill 作为局部比较器而非全局等价物。

Result: 在五项测试中，CARTOGRAPH-A 显著优于原始投影（p < 10^-21）；成功识别并撤回三个库外药代动力学机制，保留库内控制；低维场景中理论预测与实测近似平局一致；在对 40 个声明的回溯审计中，拒绝机制准确识别所有 4 个后期被判定为不确定的案例，且通过 32/36 个确认案例。

Conclusion: CARTOGRAPH 提供了一种高效、可解释且可靠的 AI 科学验证机制，能有效识别并拒绝不可靠或库外预测，显著提升科学发现的可信度与可重复性。其方法论与实证结果表明该框架适用于复杂科学系统中的安全推理与决策支持。

Abstract: We present CARTOGRAPH, a verification layer for AI scientists that couples unresolved-subspace experiment steering (select), explicit ambiguity closure (resolve), and residual-based library inadequacy detection (refuse). Under a local linear-Gaussian bridge, raw unresolved projection is the isotropic unresolved Fisher-information trace, while CARTOGRAPH-A is the exact unresolved A-optimal rule; closed-form EIG and Box-Hill arise as local comparators rather than global equivalents. Across five testbeds, CARTOGRAPH-A beats raw projection 129W/0T/15L at d = 8 (p < 10^-21) in a replicated structured cascade. More distinctively, the framework tentatively identifies three out-of-library pharmacokinetic mechanisms and then revokes those identifications as residuals expose structural misfit, while one perturbed in-library control stays identified throughout. In low-dimensional pharmacokinetic and filtered EPA settings, near-ties against disagreement are predicted by theory and observed. Finally, in a retrospective audit of 40 positive claims from the published A-Lab autonomous materials system, the refuse guard flags all 4 claims later marked inconclusive under manual reanalysis while passing 32/36 confirmed claims. Code is available at https://github.com/ai4science-boed/cartograph.git

### [115] [MST-Direct at Scale: Multivariate and Conditional Geostatistical Simulation via Sinkhorn Optimal Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07578)
*Tcharlies Bachmann Schmitz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文将MST-Direct方法从原始的双变量、无条件、小网格设置扩展到多变量、条件及大网格场景，通过稀疏候选限制的Sinkhorn匹配器解决可扩展性问题（内存复杂度O(nC)），利用独立的FFT-MA高斯骨架再现指定变异函数以实现多变量扩展，并通过克里金法对骨架进行硬数据条件化，同时保持目标数据元组的传输计划为置换，精确保留多变量联合分布。在六变量、异方差、强非线性参考分布下，无论是无条件（200x200）还是条件（100x100，200个硬数据样本）场景中，该方法均表现出零直方图误差、完全满足硬数据约束并准确再现空间相关结构，优于投影追踪多变量变换（PPMT）方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始的MST-Direct方法存在三个主要局限：难以扩展至数千个节点以上；仅限于双变量情况；无法有效处理硬数据条件化。因此需要改进以适应更复杂的实际地质统计模拟需求。

Method: 采用稀疏候选限制的Sinkhorn匹配器降低内存开销至O(nC)，引入独立的FFT-MA高斯骨架以生成多变量目标分布，并通过固定观测值位置结合克里金法对骨架进行条件化，确保运输计划为置换，从而精确保持多变量联合分布。

Result: 在六变量、异方差、强非线性条件下，无论无条件或条件情形，MST-Direct均实现零直方图误差，完全满足硬数据约束，准确再现空间相关结构，且优于作为对比的PPMT方法。

Conclusion: MST-Direct方法成功扩展至多变量、条件和大网格场景，在保持精确联合分布的同时具备良好的可扩展性和条件化能力，是高效可靠的地质统计模拟工具。

Abstract: This paper extends MST-Direct, a Matching-via-Sinkhorn-Transport approach for multivariate geostatistical simulation, from the original bivariate, unconditional, small-grid formulation to multivariate, conditional, and large-grid settings. We address the three main limitations identified in the original work: (i) scalability beyond a few thousand nodes through a sparse, candidate-restricted Sinkhorn matcher with O(nC) memory complexity; (ii) extension to multiple variables by matching target value tuples onto an independent FFT-MA Gaussian backbone that reproduces a prescribed variogram; and (iii) hard-data conditioning by fixing observed data tuples at their spatial locations while conditioning the backbone through kriging. Because the transport plan remains a permutation of the target tuples, the multivariate joint distribution is preserved exactly.
  The method is validated using the same six-variate, heteroscedastic, strongly nonlinear reference distribution employed in Direct Multivariate Simulation (DMS), under both unconditional (200x200) and conditional (100x100, 200 hard-data samples) scenarios, and is benchmarked against the Projection Pursuit Multivariate Transform (PPMT). Results show that MST-Direct reproduces the joint distribution with zero histogram error, exactly honours hard data, and accurately reproduces the prescribed spatial correlation structure, whereas PPMT remains an approximation.
  Index Terms-Optimal transport, Sinkhorn algorithm, geostatistical simulation, multivariate simulation.

### [116] [Training-Inference Kernel Contracts: Bounding Divergence in Post-Training and Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07581)
*Bruce Changlong Xu,Lan Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为'kernel contracts'的合同优先框架，用于规范训练和推理内核在有限精度下的可接受差异。该框架通过结合数值、统计、运行时和可观测性条款及违规升级策略，定义了训练（K_train）与推理（K_inf）内核之间的偏差容忍度。研究推导了从对数偏移到总变差距离再到奖励漂移的边界链，并将其应用于强化学习后训练场景，量化了单个标记的重要性比率漂移对策略梯度偏差的影响。同时介绍了四阶段上线流水线、在线路由循环和最小化YAML DSL以支持合同元数据。本文为框架与术语论文，未报告大规模实证验证结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现代强化学习后训练流程中，训练和推理使用不同的内核实现，导致相同权重下分布存在差异，尤其在低频基准测试中表现显著。这种差异可能影响模型性能与可靠性，因此需要一种机制来明确界定可接受的偏差范围。

Method: 提出'kernel contracts'框架，包含五元组结构（N, S, R, O, Pi），分别对应数值、统计、运行时、可观测性和升级策略；建立从logit drift到total-variation distance再到reward drift的理论边界链；针对强化学习后训练场景，基于重要性比值漂移推导策略梯度偏差上界；设计四阶段推广流程与在线路由系统，并提供轻量级YAML DSL用于表达合同。

Result: 成功构建了一个形式化框架，能够量化并控制训练与推理内核间的差异，为模型部署提供可解释的稳定性保障；理论分析表明，在合理假设下，单个token的重要性比率漂移可被约束，从而限制策略梯度偏差；提供了完整的合同描述语言与部署基础设施原型。

Conclusion: 本文提出的kernel contracts框架为训练与推理内核间差异提供了形式化建模与监控手段，是实现高可靠、可验证模型部署的重要基础。尽管缺乏生产规模验证，但其理论严谨性与系统设计已具备广泛适用潜力。

Abstract: A modern post-training pipeline often writes one symbol for its policy, pi_theta, while evaluating it through two different programs: a training kernel optimized for autograd and an inference kernel optimized for low-precision, fused, dynamically batched serving. In finite precision, these kernels can induce different distributions at identical weights, with the gap concentrated on slices that aggregate benchmarks under-represent. This paper proposes kernel contracts: a contract-first framework for specifying acceptable divergence between K_train and K_inf. A contract C = (N, S, R, O, Pi) combines numerical, statistical, runtime, and observability clauses with an escalation policy from violations to routing actions. We derive a chain of bounds from logit drift to total-variation distance to bounded reward drift, and specialize it to RL post-training, where per-token importance-ratio drift yields a bound on policy-gradient bias under explicit support and norm assumptions. We also describe a four-stage promotion pipeline, online routing loop, and minimal YAML DSL for contract artifacts. This is a framework and vocabulary paper; we do not report production-scale empirical validation.

</details>


### [117] [Customer Churn Prediction on Structured Data Using FT-Transformer and Stacking Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07582)
*Joyjit Roy,Samaresh Kumar Singh,Laxmi Shaw*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种融合特征标记化变压器（FT-Transformer）与梯度提升树的校准感知堆叠框架，用于结构化数据上的客户流失预测。该方法通过自注意力捕捉高阶特征交互，结合XGBoost的决策边界建模，并采用类别加权损失函数处理类别不平衡问题。通过基于留出折叠的堆叠策略和逻辑回归元学习器，实现输出校准与最优权重学习。在公开银行流失数据集上，该模型达到62.10% F1、0.861 AUC-ROC和0.647 PR-AUC，显著优于MLP基线，且具备可复现性与扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 客户流失预测在保险、数字银行、电商和订阅平台等数据驱动行业中至关重要，但受限于类别不平衡、非线性特征交互及异质特征类型，传统方法难以有效应对。现有研究存在统计验证不足、概率校准缺失和可复现性差等问题，亟需更稳健且可解释的混合模型架构。

Method: 提出一种校准感知的堆叠集成框架：使用FT-Transformer捕获高阶特征交互，结合XGBoost建模梯度提升决策边界；采用类别加权损失函数缓解类别不平衡；通过出样本折叠（OOF）堆叠与逻辑回归元学习器进行模型融合，实现输出校准与权重优化。

Result: 在公开银行流失数据集上，该混合模型在5x5交叉验证下取得62.10% F1、0.861 AUC-ROC和0.647 PR-AUC，相比MLP基线提升3.37 F1点和0.027 AUC，且95%置信区间内显著。消融实验表明，变压器组件与堆叠策略均对性能有实质性贡献。

Conclusion: 所提出的混合架构有效整合了深度学习与树模型的优势，兼顾性能、校准性和可复现性，为结构化表格数据上的客户流失预测提供了一个可扩展、可重复的先进参考范式。

Abstract: Customer churn prediction is essential across data-driven industries such as insurance, digital banking, eCommerce, and subscription platforms, where retaining existing customers is typically more cost-effective than acquiring new ones. Predicting churn on structured datasets remains challenging due to class imbalance, nonlinear feature interactions, and heterogeneous feature types. Tree-based ensemble methods consistently demonstrate strong performance in these contexts, often outperforming conventional neural networks. This study introduces a validated hybrid architecture that integrates feature-tokenized transformers (FT-Transformer) with gradient-boosted trees through calibration-aware stacking. The proposed framework addresses persistent gaps in statistical validation, probability calibration, and reproducibility found in prior research. The FT-Transformer captures higher-order feature interactions using self-attention, while XGBoost captures gradient-boosted decision boundaries with complementary inductive biases. Class imbalance is handled using class-weighted loss functions, thereby avoiding synthetic oversampling and preserving minority-class distributions. The models are ensembled using out-of-fold (OOF) stacking with a logistic regression meta-learner, which recalibrates overconfident base model outputs and learns optimal combination weights. On a public bank churn dataset, the hybrid model achieves 62.10% F1, 0.861 AUC-ROC, and 0.647 PR-AUC, outperforming the Multi-Layer Perceptron (MLP) baseline by 3.37 F1 points and 0.027 AUC under 5x5 cross-validation with 95% confidence intervals reported. Ablation studies demonstrate that both the transformer component and stacking strategy contribute materially to performance. The proposed methodology offers a reproducible and extensible reference architecture for contemporary churn prediction on structured tabular data.

</details>

### [120] [The Routing Plateau: Understanding and Breaking the Accuracy Limits of LLM Routers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07587)
*Yifan Lu,Qiyue Zhang,Shenrun Zhang,Zhibo Yu,Zhuang Wang,Hanjie Chen,Jiarong Xing*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对21种路由方法在五个基准上进行系统评估，分析性能趋同现象；通过实验探究可预测性瓶颈的成因，并测试不同改进策略（如更大数据集、更强编码器、端到端微调）的效果。

Conclusion: 当前路由方法受制于可预测性瓶颈，未来应聚焦于建模查询特定的细粒度信号，通过更大规模数据、更强模型和端到端优化来突破性能平台。

Abstract: LLM routing has become a popular approach to improve the cost-quality trade-off of LLM services by dynamically selecting a model for each query. Recent work has explored a broad range of routing methods, including clustering-based routers, learned classifiers, pairwise ranking, and confidence-based approaches. Our extensive study of 21 routing methods across five benchmarks reveals a consistent phenomenon that we call the routing plateau: many methods, including kNN, achieve very similar accuracy and converge to a narrow performance range that remains far below the oracle router. Our investigation shows that the plateau is largely caused by a predictability bottleneck: current routers mainly learn global averaged model-performance trends rather than fine-grained query-specific routing signals. As a result, they solve overlapping easy queries but collectively fail on hard queries that require instance-specific routing decisions. We further study how to move beyond the plateau and find that larger training datasets, stronger encoders, and end-to-end fine-tuning can further improve routing accuracy. These findings characterize the common limits of current routing methods and provide insights and actionable directions for the community to build more effective routing systems.

### [123] [UNIQ: Conformal Calibration for Adaptive Conservatism in Offline Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07592)
*Aditya Upadhyay*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: UNIQ 是一种基于隐式 Q 学习（IQL）的离线强化学习方法，通过分位数校准的不确定性估计实现状态自适应的保守性。它使用多期望值价值集成，结合分割置信预测计算分布无关的不确定性，并将该信号映射为状态相关的期望值，在数据覆盖良好的区域放松保守性，而在数据边界附近的不确定区域增强保守性。在 D4RL MuJoCo 基准上，UNIQ 持续优于 IQL，尤其在 Walker2d 和高重放任务中表现显著；同时其内存开销仅约 250MB，比 EDAC 降低约 10 倍。本文强调其作为实用机制的贡献，提升离线 RL 中性能与效率的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有离线强化学习方法对所有状态采用固定的保守惩罚，忽视了局部数据覆盖率的差异，导致在数据丰富区域过度保守、在数据稀疏区域保守不足。需要一种能根据状态局部数据覆盖情况自适应调整保守性的机制。

Method: 基于 IQL 骨干，训练多期望值价值集成；利用分割置信预测生成分布无关的不确定性估计；将不确定性信号映射为状态依赖的期望值，实现自适应保守性调节。

Result: 在 D4RL MuJoCo 基准上，UNIQ 显著优于 IQL，尤其在 Walker2d 及高重放任务中提升明显；峰值显存约 250MB，相比 EDAC 有约 10 倍的内存优化。

Conclusion: UNIQ 提供了一种高效且实用的自适应保守机制，有效改善了离线强化学习中的性能-效率权衡，而非追求整体性能最优。

Abstract: Offline reinforcement learning requires careful conservatism to mitigate distribution shift, yet most existing methods apply a fixed penalty uniformly across all states regardless of local data coverage. We present UNIQ (Uncertainty-Informed Quantile), an offline RL method that introduces state-adaptive conservatism through conformally calibrated uncertainty estimation. Built on the Implicit Q-Learning (IQL) backbone, UNIQ trains a multi-expectile value ensemble, computes distribution-free uncertainty estimates using split conformal prediction, and maps the resulting signal to a state-dependent expectile that relaxes conservatism in well-covered regions while strengthening it in uncertain regions near the data frontier. On D4RL MuJoCo benchmarks, UNIQ consistently improves over IQL, with the largest gains observed on Walker2d and replay-heavy tasks. At the same time, UNIQ operates at near-IQL memory cost (approximately 250 MB peak VRAM), providing roughly a 10x reduction compared to EDAC. Rather than pursuing overall state-of-the-art performance, we position UNIQ as a practical mechanism contribution that improves the performance-efficiency trade-off in offline reinforcement learning.

### [124] [Shortcuts in the Tail: Debiasing via Post-Hoc Spectral Compression of Fine-Tuning Updates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07596)
*Edward Sun,Dmitrii Troitskii*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种简单的后处理干预方法，通过截断微调前后权重差矩阵ΔW的奇异值分解（SVD）尾部，有效减少模型对伪相关性的依赖，且无需重新训练、分组标签或人工构造反事实数据。该方法在多个指令微调模型和分类基准上均显著降低少数群体的性能差距，同时保持任务准确率损失小于2个百分点，尤其在CivilComments数据集上效果提升达5倍。研究发现，伪相关响应位于ΔW的奇异值尾部，表明ΔW的奇异基构成了一种可解释微调学习内容的坐标系。控制实验排除了低秩近似等其他解释，支持该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微调过程中常引入与任务无关的伪相关性，导致模型在少数群体上表现系统性下降。现有缓解方法存在重训练、需分组标签或依赖人工反事实数据等局限，因此亟需一种无需额外数据或训练的后处理策略。

Method: 通过计算微调权重与基础权重的差值矩阵ΔW = W_ft - W_base，对其执行奇异值分解（SVD），并截断奇异值的尾部（top-k truncation），实现对伪相关性的抑制。该方法为后处理操作，不涉及模型再训练或外部标注。

Result: 在三个不同规模的指令微调模型（0.5B–7B）和四个分类任务上，该方法在所有测试条件下均降低了少数群体的性能差距，且平均准确率损失低于2个百分点；在CivilComments数据集上，性能差距改善幅度最高达5倍。控制实验表明，该效果并非源于低秩近似或随机截断等通用机制。

Conclusion: ΔW的奇异基提供了一个有效的坐标系统，可用于分析微调过程中学习到的内容。截断其尾部成分是一种高效、轻量级的后处理方法，能有效缓解伪相关性问题，具有广泛适用性与可扩展性。

Abstract: Fine-tuning often introduces spurious correlations alongside task knowledge, causing systematic failures on underrepresented groups. Existing mitigations require retraining, group labels, or curated counterfactual data. We show a simple post-hoc intervention reduces shortcut reliance without any of these: truncating the tail of the SVD of $ΔW = W_\mathrm{ft} - W_\mathrm{base}$ reduces the spurious-group gap while preserving task accuracy. Across three instruction-tuned models ($0.5$B--$7$B) and four classification benchmarks, top-$k$ truncation reduces the gap on every cell at $<2$ pp accuracy loss, by up to $5\times$ on CivilComments. We propose this works because the shortcut response sits in the tail of the singular ordering of $ΔW$, a claim about how truncation behaves rather than about the raw singular values, which are broadly distributed and look the same across all four datasets. A controlled boundary case in which fine-tuning has only a shortcut to learn shows the predicted FT-to-base collapse, and bottom-/random-$k$ and matched-rank LoRA controls rule out generic low-rank approximation and rank-constrained training as the explanation. We read this as preliminary evidence that the singular basis of $ΔW$ is a useful coordinate system for studying what fine-tuning has learned.

### [125] [Repetition Mismatch: Why Data Mixture Experiments Don't Scale and How to Fix Them](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07597)
*Kevin Zhou,Lisa Alazraki,Kris Cao,Marek Rei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了预训练数据混合在大规模训练中的优化问题，指出小规模实验难以泛化的主要原因是高质数据重复率随训练预算变化导致的重复不匹配。通过引入与目标重复率一致的子采样方法，仅需1/16的训练量即可接近最优混合比例，显著优于传统方法。该方法在多源数据场景下依然有效，表明数据重复应作为混合优化中的核心变量对待。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当高质量数据稀缺且需要重复使用时，传统的小规模实验无法准确预测大规模训练下的最优数据混合比例，主要因为重复率随训练预算变化而改变，导致小规模实验结果不可靠。

Method: 提出一种基于目标重复率的子采样方法，确保小规模实验中的数据重复率与最终目标一致，从而消除重复不匹配的影响。

Result: 在两源数据设置中，仅用1/16的训练数据即可获得接近最优的混合比例（误差0.05），而传统方法误差达0.75；在三源数据中，两个重复控制实验即可找到最优混合，远优于需完整训练多个实验的基线方法。

Conclusion: 重复动态是影响小规模实验泛化能力的关键因素，而非单纯训练规模。数据重复应被视为混合优化中的第一类变量，而非次要副作用。

Abstract: Pre-training data mixtures are commonly tuned by running small-scale experiments and extrapolating to the target training budget. When high-quality data is scarce and must be repeated, this extrapolation frequently fails, but the source of the failure has not been isolated. We show that a primary culprit is a repetition mismatch: because high-quality datasets are small, their repetition rate changes as the training budget grows, shifting the optimal mixture in ways that small-scale proxy experiments do not anticipate. A subsampling procedure that matches the target repetition rate controls for this effect. In a two-source setting combining limited high-quality data with web crawl, a single repetition-controlled experiment using only 1/16 of the target tokens recovers a mixture within 0.05 of the optimum for a 757M parameter model, compared to an error of 0.75 without repetition control. Achieving comparable accuracy without repetition control requires three to four horizons, consuming 44 to 94% of the target token budget. With three data sources, the larger mixture space requires more than a single experiment to constrain, but the approach remains effective: at the 757M scale, just two repetition-controlled horizons recover the optimal mixture, outperforming baselines that instead require the full two-source experiments to construct. Our results reveal that repetition dynamics, not scale alone, shape whether small-scale mixture experiments generalize. More broadly, they suggest that data repetition deserves treatment as a first-class variable in mixture optimization, rather than an inconvenient side effect of limited data.

</details>


### [126] [A Topological Characterization of Graph Neural Networks via Stochastic Block Model Embeddings on the n-Sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07598)
*Gopal Anantharaman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种拓扑框架，用于比较训练好的图神经网络（GNN），通过将消息传递神经网络（MPNN）在图核-信号空间上诱导的随机块模型（SBM）映射到单位n-球面$\sphere^{n-1}\subset\R^n$。该方法基于三个经典理论：图核空间的紧性、Frieze-Kannan弱正则性引理及其图核-信号扩展，以及MPNN对切距离的Lipschitz连续性。研究证明，对于任意给定容差$\varepsilon>0$，一个训练好的MPNN在足够大的图上可近似分解为复杂度受限的分段图核-信号，并构造了一个保测映射$Ψ_n$，将SBM区域置于不相交的球帽上。这生成了无需特定任务的低维“指纹”，可用于可视化和跨模型库的最近邻搜索，实现无需重训练的迁移学习候选检索。文章还讨论了高维集中现象对大规模模型嵌入的影响，并提出了五个未来研究方向：双曲与格拉斯曼流形替代方案、基于图核-信号的Gromov-Wasserstein距离、信息几何（Fisher）重构、层间嵌入云的持久同调指纹，以及基于图核特征分解的谱距离基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以有效比较和检索训练好的图神经网络，尤其在大规模模型中缺乏通用且可解释的表示方式。本文旨在构建一种问题无关的低维拓扑表示，以支持模型间的可视化比较与高效检索，推动迁移学习的应用。

Method: 结合图核空间的紧性、弱正则性引理及其扩展，利用MPNN对切距离的Lipschitz性质，构造保测映射将SBM区域嵌入单位球面，形成低维指纹；并引入多种潜在改进路径如双曲结构、信息几何等。

Result: 成功构造出问题无关的低维“指纹”表示，可实现训练后GNN的可视化与最近邻搜索，支持迁移学习候选检索；揭示了高维集中现象对大模型嵌入的挑战；提出多个可拓展的研究方向。

Conclusion: 该拓扑框架为训练后的图神经网络提供了一种通用、可解释且高效的比较机制，具备良好的应用前景，特别是在大规模模型管理和迁移学习中。同时，其理论基础与扩展潜力为后续研究提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: We propose a topological framework for comparing trained Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) by mapping the Stochastic Block Models (SBMs) induced on the graphon-signal space of a Message Passing Neural Network (MPNN) onto the unit $n$-sphere $\sphere^{n-1}\subset\R^n$. The construction rests on three classical pillars: the \emph{compactness} of the cut-distance graphon space $(\Wo,\cutdist)$ \citep{lovasz2006limits,lovasz2012large}, the Frieze--Kannan \emph{weak regularity lemma} together with its graphon-signal extension due to \citet{levie2023graphon}, and the Lipschitz continuity of MPNNs with respect to the cut-distance. We show that, for any prescribed tolerance $\varepsilon>0$, a trained MPNN $Φ$ acting on a sufficiently large graph factors (up to $\varepsilon$) through a step-graphon-signal of bounded complexity, and we construct an explicit measure-preserving map $Ψ_n\colon[0,1]\to\sphere^{n-1}$ that places the SBM regions on disjoint spherical caps. This produces a problem-agnostic, low-dimensional ``fingerprint'' of a trained GNN that is amenable to visual inspection and to nearest-neighbour search across model zoos, enabling \emph{transfer-learning candidate retrieval} without retraining. We discuss the obstruction posed by concentration of measure in high dimension -- a phenomenon directly relevant to LLM-scale embeddings. We close with five concrete future research directions: hyperbolic and Grassmannian alternatives to the spherical model, Gromov--Wasserstein distances on graphon-signals as an isometry-free alternative to the $n$-sphere map, an information-geometric (Fisher) reformulation of the SBM manifold, persistent-homology fingerprints of layer-wise embedding clouds, and a spectral-distance baseline derived from the graphon eigendecomposition.

### [127] [DiffoR: A Unified Continuous Generative Framework for Universal Ordinal Regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07599)
*Hongxu Ma,Lin Wang,Chenghou Jin,Han Zhou,Jie Zhang,Xiaoyu Yang,Chunjie Chen,Jihong Guan,Shuigeng Zhou*

Method: 提出连续生成型序数回归框架DiffOR，利用扩散模型进行迭代去噪以恢复连续序数值；设计双解耦策略：空间上多尺度增量聚合分解目标，时间上动态去噪感知同步去噪步与特征频率，实现精细建模。

Conclusion: DiffOR通过连续生成范式与双解耦策略，有效克服传统方法的局限，实现了更强的表征能力、可解释性与泛化性能，为序数回归提供了新范式。

Abstract: Ordinal Regression (OR) aims to predict target values with inherent order, underpinning critical applications across diverse domains, from recommender systems to computer vision. Though having evolved from naive regression to discretization-based classification and generation, existing paradigms remain fundamentally constrained by quantization artifacts and the lack of global ordinal topological perception. These methods typically enforce rigid boundary delineations, failing to capture the non-stationary semantic transitions inherent to ordinal data. In this paper, we propose a novel paradigm where OR is formulated as a Continuous Generative Ordinal Regression task. Under the novel paradigm, we introduce DiffOR, a unified framework that leverages diffusion models to recover continuous ordinal values via iterative denoising, thereby enabling the dynamic learning of soft semantic transitions. To explicitly preserve ordinal topology, we devise a Dual-Decoupling Strategy: Spatially, Multi-scale Increment Aggregation decomposes targets into hierarchical continuous increments; Temporally, Dynamic Denoising Perception synchronizes denoising steps with feature frequencies, ensuring robust coarse-to-fine refinement. Theoretically, we show that the proposed method can significantly enhance both representation capability and mechanistic interpretability. Extensive experiments on 12 benchmarks across four domains validate DiffOR's consistent superiority over state-of-the-art methods, establishing a new standard that demonstrates strong potential as a general-purpose solution for universal ordinal regression.

### [128] [Reachability and asymptotics of Gaussian Transformer dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07600)
*Albert Alcalde,Zhengping Ji,Enrique Zuazua*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将Transformer中的数据传播建模为概率测度空间上的非线性控制系统。针对带有自注意力和仿射前馈层的均值场Transformer模型，证明了高斯分布沿其诱导流保持精确高斯性，从而将无限维测度动力学简化为有限维双线性控制系统，描述均值与协方差的演化。该框架将Transformer的表达能力转化为对指定高斯矩的可达性问题，并揭示其与经典滤波与控制中Riccati型方程的新联系。对于时变控制，证明了在初始协方差秩不变的前提下，可精确实现任意目标高斯分布的有限时间可达性；对于时不变参数，给出了导致渐近稳定或有限时间协方差爆破的显式谱条件。数值实验验证了实际Transformer在早期和中间层中输入为高斯时仍保持接近矩匹配的高斯分布，且预设注意力矩阵的模型准确再现了预测的协方差演化行为：稳定配置下有界演化，不稳定配置下发生爆破。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将Transformer的数据传播形式化为概率测度空间上的非线性控制系统；利用均值场近似处理自注意力与前馈层；通过数学分析证明高斯分布的不变性；推导出均值与协方差的双线性控制系统；结合控制理论工具研究可达性、稳定性与爆破行为；通过数值实验验证理论结果在真实Transformer中的表现。

Result: 1. 高斯分布沿Transformer流保持精确高斯性，实现无限维测度动力学向有限维双线性系统的降维；2. 时变控制下，任意目标高斯分布可在有限时间内被达到，前提是其协方差秩与初始一致；3. 时不变参数下，存在明确的谱条件决定系统是否趋于正定平衡点或发生有限时间协方差爆破；4. 数值实验表明，实际Transformer在高斯输入下维持近似高斯分布，且注意力结构决定了协方差演化模式（稳定或爆破）。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了Transformer数据传播与非线性控制理论之间的深刻联系，揭示了高斯分布的内在不变性及其对表达能力与稳定性的深远影响。该框架不仅为理解模型动态提供了统一的数学语言，也为设计更稳定、可预测的Transformer架构提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We formulate data propagation through the Transformer, the machine learning architecture powering large language models, as a nonlinear control system on the space of probability measures. For the mean-field Transformer model with self-attention and affine feed-forward layers, we prove that Gaussian distributions remain exactly Gaussian along the induced flow. This invariance reduces the infinite-dimensional measure dynamics to a finite-dimensional bilinear control system governing the evolution of the mean and covariance, reformulates the expressive capacity of Transformers as a reachability problem for prescribed Gaussian moments, and reveals a novel connection with Riccati-type equations from classical filtering and control.
  For time-varying controls, we prove exact finite-time reachability of any target Gaussian distribution whose covariance matrix has the same rank as the initial one, this rank constraint being an intrinsic invariant of the dynamics. For time-invariant parameters, we derive explicit spectral conditions leading either to asymptotic stability toward positive-definite equilibria or to finite-time blow-up of the covariance.
  Numerical experiments complement the theory by showing that practical Transformers with Gaussian inputs remain close to moment-matched Gaussian distributions through early and intermediate layers, while Transformers with prescribed attention matrices reproduce the predicted covariance regimes: bounded evolution in stabilizing configurations and blow-up in destabilizing ones.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计双分支架构，分别建模瞬态与稳态动态；融合拉普拉斯与傅里叶变换的谱特性，实现对系统动态的显式分解与联合学习。

We evaluate LFNO on nine benchmarks, including three ODE systems (Duffing, Lorenz, and Pendulum) and six PDE systems (Euler-Bernoulli beam, Heat, Reaction-diffusion, Brusselator, Burgers, and Navier-Stokes). LFNO significantly outperforms existing operators on ODE systems, where transient dynamics dominate, and consistently surpasses LNO while achieving performance competitive with FNO on PDE benchmarks. Furthermore, LFNO offers improved stability and physical interpretability through its component-wise decomposition. These results demonstrate that LFNO provides a robust and unified approach for learning complex dynamical systems across multiple temporal scales.

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为SRT的新框架，用于时间序列的超分辨率重建。该方法通过解耦的修正流分解趋势与季节性成分，利用隐式神经表示对齐至目标分辨率，并引入跨分辨率注意力机制生成高分辨率细节。此外，还提出了SRT-large模型，具备强大的零样本超分辨率能力。在九个公开数据集上的实验表明，SRT及其扩展版本在多种缩放因子下均优于现有方法，验证了其鲁棒性和各组件的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高分辨率时间序列数据对于精确分析至关重要，但其获取受成本和可行性限制。现有图像超分辨率技术难以直接应用于时间序列，因此需要一种专门针对时间序列特性的超分辨率方法。

Method: SRT框架首先将输入时间序列分解为趋势和季节性成分；然后使用隐式神经表示将这些成分对齐到目标分辨率；最后通过跨分辨率注意力机制引导高分辨率细节的生成。SRT-large则通过大规模预训练实现了零样本超分辨率能力。

Result: 在九个公共数据集上，SRT和SRT-large在多个缩放因子下均显著优于现有方法，展现出优异的性能和组件有效性。

Conclusion: SRT及其扩展版本SRT-large为时间序列超分辨率提供了一个高效且可扩展的解决方案，证明了其在不同场景下的鲁棒性和先进性。

Abstract: Fine-grained time series data with high temporal resolution is critical for accurate analytics across a wide range of applications. However, the acquisition of such data is often limited by cost and feasibility. This problem can be tackled by reconstructing high-resolution signals from low-resolution inputs based on specific priors, known as super-resolution. While extensively studied in computer vision, directly transferring image super-resolution techniques to time series is not trivial. To address this challenge at a fundamental level, we propose Super-Resolution for Time series (SRT), a novel framework that reconstructs temporal patterns lost in low-resolution inputs via disentangled rectified flow. SRT decomposes the input into trend and seasonal components, aligns them to the target resolution using an implicit neural representation, and leverages a novel cross-resolution attention mechanism to guide the generation of high-resolution details. We further introduce SRT-large, a scaled-up version with extensive pre-training, which enables strong zero-shot super-resolution capability. Extensive experiments on nine public datasets demonstrate that SRT and SRT-large consistently outperform existing methods across multiple scale factors, showing both robust performance and the effectiveness of each component in our architecture.

### [134] [QDSP: An Interpretable Structured Learning Framework for Predicting Death or Cerebral Palsy in Very Low Birth Weight Infants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07606)

The QSS module constructs stability-aware and low-redundancy feature subspaces through bootstrap-based feature consistency estimation, whereas the DSP module employs differentiable soft oblique decision structures to model nonlinear clinical interactions while preserving traceable decision evidence. In addition, SHAP-based analyses and differentiable decision-path tracing identified clinically relevant predictors, including cystic periventricular leukomalacia (cPVL) and birth weight, consistent with established neonatal pathophysiological evidence. These results suggest that QDSP provides an interpretable and robust framework for discharge-time risk stratification in VLBWI and may support early individualized clinical decision-making in neonatal intensive care settings.

Abstract: Advances in machine learning and computational power have unlocked the predictive potential of the human genome, yet biologists now demand that these models also elucidate the underlying biological mechanisms. Through a benchmarking study on transcription factor binding, we demonstrate the risks of current practices. We show that different IML methods can often (1) yield contradictory explanations for the same predictions, (2) fail to localize known regulatory motifs, and (3) fail to faithfully reflect the model's internal decision process. In light of this, we argue for a validation framework analogous to clinical trials: just as trials require rigorous design and adverse-event reporting, genomic interpretability must move beyond cherry-picked plausibility toward systematic assessment of consistency, faithfulness, and biological validity. ### [136] [LEAF: Growing Trees Without Branching for Speech-Aware Large Language Model Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07610)
*Argyrios Gerogiannis,Yekaterina Yegorova,Mark Hasegawa-Johnson,Venugopal V. Veeravalli*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LEAF提出一种基于回溯树的强化学习方法，通过恢复响应中的共享前缀结构，实现细粒度的跨度级信用分配，无需在线分支或额外解码。它在语音问答和语音翻译任务上优于GRPO方法，并且小规模模型表现超过当前全参数基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GRPO风格方法在语音感知大语言模型后训练中存在粗粒度信用分配问题，将相同的终端奖励优势广播给响应中的每个词元，忽略了响应批次内语音条件生成中常见的共享前缀结构，导致关键决策点信息丢失。

Method: LEAF通过采样完整响应，选择高意外性边界，按共享前缀对响应分组，并利用后代奖励进行跨度级优势分配，实现回溯式树结构建模。

Result: 在相同采样和低秩适配预算下，LEAF在语音问答和语音翻译任务上均优于GRPO；更小的LEAF模型性能超越当前最先进的全参数基线模型。

Conclusion: LEAF通过恢复响应内部结构，实现了更精准的信用分配，在资源受限条件下显著提升性能，证明了其在语音感知语言模型后训练中的有效性与高效性。

Abstract: State-of-the-art GRPO-style methods for speech-aware large language model post-training suffer from coarse credit assignment, broadcasting the same terminal-reward advantage to every token in a response. This ignores useful structure within rollout batches, where speech-conditioned completions often share prefixes before diverging at important decisions. We propose Low-rank Exploration with Adaptive Forking (LEAF), a retrospective tree-based RL method that recovers this structure without online branching or additional decoding. LEAF samples complete responses, selects high-surprisal boundaries, groups responses by shared prefixes, and assigns span-level advantages using descendant rewards. We theoretically justify LEAF's span-level credit assignment and boundary-selection design. Empirically, LEAF improves over GRPO across speech question answering and speech translation benchmarks under the same rollout and low-rank adaptation budget. Notably, smaller LEAF-trained models outperform current state-of-the-art, full-parameter baselines.

</details>


### [137] [Measuring Poverty and Inequality with Reduced Data: A Machine Learning Approach Using Nigerian Household Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07614)

Abstract: Reliable measurement of income and consumption is essential for monitoring poverty and inequality in low- and middle-income countries, yet full household surveys are costly and difficult to implement regularly. This paper examines whether reduced survey instruments can preserve key distributional information. We apply Random Forest Recursive Feature Elimination (RF-RFE) to the 2018/19 Nigeria General Household Survey-Panel to identify the income sources, consumption categories and household characteristics that best classify individuals within the welfare distribution. The analysis focuses on three outcomes: poverty status, location in the quintile distribution and position relative to the Gini-based inequality line. The survey's post-planting and post-harvest periods allow us to assess performance under different seasonal contexts. Results show that RF-RFE achieves strong classification accuracy with few predictors. For consumption, poverty status and inequality-line position are accurately predicted using a small set of expenditure categories, while quintile classification reaches about 80 percent accuracy for seasonal consumption and 60--65 percent for annual consumption predicted from a single seasonal visit. For income, poverty status reaches around 90 percent accuracy with five predictors, and inequality-line position is largely captured by labour earnings. The findings suggest that machine-learning methods can help improve survey design and reduce data requirements while retaining much of the distributional information needed to measure and monitor poverty and inequality.

### [138] [Structured Neuron Pruning in Deep Neural Networks Using Multi-Armed Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07615)
*Salem Ameen,Sunil Vadera*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种基于多臂赌博机（MAB）算法的结构化神经元剪枝框架，通过将每个候选神经元视为一个‘臂’，利用多种策略（如UCB1、Thompson Sampling等）评估并移除冗余神经元，实现模型压缩。实验表明，在分类、回归及深度学习任务中，该方法显著优于未剪枝模型和传统剪枝方法，具有良好的性能与计算可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度神经网络中存在大量冗余隐藏单元，传统权重剪枝导致非结构化稀疏，难以在标准密集实现中高效利用。因此需要一种能够系统性移除完整神经元的结构化剪枝方法，以实现更高效的模型压缩和推理加速。

Method: 提出基于多臂赌博机（MAB）的结构化剪枝框架，将每个神经元视为一个臂；通过临时屏蔽神经元、测量损失变化并更新其被安全移除的奖励估计，采用Epsilon-Greedy、Softmax、UCB1、Thompson Sampling、Hedge-style乘法权重和EXP3等多种策略进行选择。

Result: 在表格分类任务中，UCB1获得最高平均排名，并优于未剪枝模型；在回归任务中，UCB1表现优异，与主流回归模型相当或更优（以R^2衡量）；在深度学习任务中，UCB1和Thompson Sampling表现最佳，多个MAB策略显著超越未剪枝模型、基于幅度的剪枝和贪婪激活变化剪枝。

Conclusion: MAB-based神经元剪枝是一种有效且计算上可行的结构化模型压缩方法，可在多种任务中实现显著性能提升与模型简化。

Abstract: Deep neural networks often contain redundant hidden units. Removing individual weights can reduce parameter count, but unstructured sparsity is not always easy to exploit in standard dense implementations. This paper develops a structured pruning framework in which complete neurons are removed using multi-armed bandit (MAB) algorithms. Each candidate neuron is treated as an arm; pulling an arm temporarily masks that neuron, measures the change in loss on a sampled mini-batch, restores the neuron, and updates an estimate of its safe-removal reward. The framework supports stochastic policies, including Epsilon-Greedy, Softmax, UCB1 and Thompson Sampling, and multiplicative-weight policies, including Hedge-style multiplicative weights and EXP3. We evaluate the method on tabular classification, tabular regression and deep neural-network benchmarks covering image, text and reasoning tasks. Statistical comparisons using the Friedman test followed by the Nemenyi post-hoc test show significant differences between methods. On tabular classification tasks, UCB1 obtains the highest mean rank among pruning policies and improves on the unpruned neural network. On regression tasks, UCB1 obtains the highest mean rank and is statistically competitive with, or superior to, several standard regression models according to R^2. On deep-learning tasks, UCB1 and Thompson Sampling obtain the strongest ranks, and several MAB policies significantly outperform the unpruned model, magnitude-based neuron pruning and greedy activation-variation pruning. The results show that MAB-based neuron pruning is an effective and computationally practical approach for structured model reduction.

### [139] [Item Response Scaling Laws: A Measurement Theory Approach for Efficient and Generalizable Neural Scaling Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07616)
*Sang Truong,Yuheng Tu,Rylan Schaeffer,Sanmi Koyejo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Item Response Scaling Laws (IRSL)框架，结合项目反应理论（IRT）与缩放定律，将模型能力与题目特征解耦，将参数复杂度从O(M×N)降低到O(M+N)，显著减少计算成本。采用Beta-IRT方法，利用语言模型的响应概率（如预训练中的词元概率或测试时的通过率）捕捉更丰富的信号。在两种缩放范式下验证：(1) 预训练下游缩放，使用6,612个检查点和37,682个问题；(2) 测试时缩放，使用12个模型和120个问题，每题最多2,500次采样。仅需50个问题/基准即可获得可靠估计，相比传统方法减少99.9%评估量，且性能预测准确。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统缩放定律估计需要大量昂贵的模型-基准对评估，效率低且难以扩展。本文旨在通过引入项目反应理论（IRT），实现模型能力和题目特征的解耦，从而大幅降低计算开销并提升可扩展性。

Method: 提出IRSL框架，将缩放定律与项目反应理论结合，使用Beta-IRT建模语言模型的非二元响应（如概率输出），实现对模型能力与题目难度的联合建模，通过最小化观测响应与模型预测之间的差异来估计参数。

Result: 在多个基准上，仅需50个问题即可获得与传统方法相当甚至更优的缩放估计精度，计算成本降低99.9%；所估计的模型能力具有跨基准泛化能力，可用于性能预测。

Conclusion: IRSL提供了一种高效、可扩展的缩放定律估计方法，通过解耦模型能力与题目特征，显著降低评估成本，并具备良好的泛化能力，适用于大规模语言模型的性能分析与预测。

Abstract: Scaling laws provide a fundamental framework for understanding the performance of Language Models (LMs), yet deriving them requires prohibitively expensive evaluations across thousands of checkpoints or millions of inference samples. To address this, we introduce Item Response Scaling Laws (IRSL), a unified framework that integrates Item Response Theory (IRT) within the scaling law framework. Unlike traditional approaches that treat each model-benchmark pair in isolation, IRSL disentangles latent model ability from question characteristics, factorizing the scaling law estimation for $M$ models and $N$ questions to significantly reduce parameter complexity from $O(M \times N)$ to $O(M + N)$. We instantiate IRSL with Beta-IRT, which leverages the empirical probability responses of LMs -- such as token probabilities in pre-training and pass rates in test-time sampling -- to capture richer signals than binary responses. We validate our approach across two prevalent scaling paradigms: (1) pre-training downstream scaling, using 6,612 LM checkpoints and 37,682 questions from 10 benchmarks; and (2) test-time scaling, using 12 LMs and 120 questions from 4 benchmarks with up to 2,500 samples per question. Given a one-time calibration on existing model responses, IRSL yields more reliable scaling estimates using only 50 questions per benchmark (a 99.9\% reduction), achieving comparable or superior decision accuracy to traditional approaches. Furthermore, we show that the estimated latent model abilities are generalizable, enabling accurate performance forecasting across benchmarks that share the same measurement objective.

</details>


### [140] [Query Lens: Interpreting Sparse Key-Value Features with Indirect Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07617)
*Hwiyeong Lee,Ingyu Bang,Uiji Hwang,Hyelim Lim,Taeuk Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Query Lens extends Logit Lens to better interpret sparse autoencoder features by analyzing both encoder-side key features and decoder-side value features, capturing direct and indirect effects through downstream modules. It reveals coherent token signatures for previously uninterpretable features and introduces the Subspace Channel Hypothesis, proposing that downstream modules access features via layer-specific subspaces.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Sparse autoencoders produce more interpretable features than individual neurons, but reliably characterizing these features remains difficult. Existing methods like Logit Lens only capture direct effects, missing indirect, module-mediated influences.

Method: Query Lens jointly examines encoder-side keys and decoder-side values to identify inputs activating a feature and outputs it promotes. It also accounts for indirect effects caused by downstream modules, enabling a more comprehensive interpretation.

Result: Query Lens successfully generates coherent token signatures for features previously uninterpretable under Logit Lens, demonstrating improved interpretability and fidelity.

Conclusion: The Subspace Channel Hypothesis is proposed, suggesting that downstream modules read sparse features through layer-specific subspaces, offering new insights into how features are utilized across network layers.

Abstract: While sparse autoencoders provide features more interpretable than individual neurons, reliably characterizing them remains challenging. We propose Query Lens, which extends Logit Lens to enable more comprehensive and faithful interpretations of sparse features. By jointly considering encoder-side key features and decoder-side value features, we identify both the inputs that activate a feature and the outputs it promotes. We also account for indirect, module-mediated effects that arise when the feature is processed by downstream modules, going beyond the direct effect captured by Logit Lens. In experiments, we find that Query Lens yields coherent token signatures for features that remain uninterpretable under Logit Lens. Finally, we propose the Subspace Channel Hypothesis, suggesting that downstream modules read features through layer-specific subspaces.

</details>

*Li Lin,Xiaojun Wan*

Main category: cs.LG

Method: 提出ScaleSweep方法，通过系统性搜索满足理论边界内的块尺度候选，选择使目标误差最小的方案，并基于理论推导约束搜索范围以降低计算开销。
