Method: 将地理空间表示为异构图，融合多尺度图神经网络与球谐函数位置编码，通过对比学习对齐图嵌入与位置编码，实现从地图拓扑中学习全球位置表征。

Result: OSMGraphCLIP 在多数下游任务中性能媲美或超过卫星基线，尤其在社会经济与公共健康任务中显著领先；在生态与环境任务中仍具竞争力，且无需任何遥感数据。

Conclusion: 仅使用开放的结构化地图数据（如 OSM）即可生成高质量、跨域通用的地理表征，表明地图拓扑本身蕴含丰富的地理语义信息，可用于多种地理相关任务，具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: We present OSMGraphCLIP, a CLIP-style geospatial representation model that learns global location embeddings from freely available OpenStreetMap (OSM) data. OSMGraphCLIP represents geographic environments as heterogeneous graphs of typed OSM features, preserving the topological and semantic relationships among roads, buildings, land-use regions, and points of interest. A multi-scale graph encoder captures both fine-grained local structure and broader landscape composition, and supervises a spherical-harmonics location encoder through a contrastive alignment objective. We evaluate OSMGraphCLIP across a diverse suite of downstream geospatial regression and classification tasks spanning climate, ecology, socioeconomic indicators, public health, land cover, biodiversity, and wildfire forecasting, and show that structured OSM data alone supports strong global location representations across domains. OSMGraphCLIP matches or exceeds satellite-based baselines on the majority of benchmarks, with the most pronounced advantage on socioeconomic and public-health tasks, where OSM's explicit semantic annotation of the built environment encodes patterns of human activity that satellite pixels can only capture indirectly. On ecological and environmental tasks, the model remains closely competitive with imagery-based methods despite using no Earth observation data. Qualitative analysis confirms that the learned embeddings organize geographic space coherently, recovering biome boundaries, urban gradients, and tropical--temperate distinctions from map topology alone.

</details>


### [188] [SKILL.nb: Selective Formalization and Gated Execution for Durable Agent Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08049)
*Amine El Hattami,Nicolas Chapados,Christopher Pal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SKILL.nb 是一个用于管理可重用智能体工作流的框架，通过证据校准的生命周期策略提升可靠性。它采用选择性形式化：根据执行证据决定哪些步骤应转为可执行代码，哪些保持自然语言引导，并在必要时修订决策。工作流以可审计、版本化的笔记本形式存储，融合自然语言指导、多语言可执行单元、验证门控、回退路径和多模态证据（如输出、截图、错误追踪）。运行时，仅在门控条件满足时执行代码，否则本地回退。在 WebArena-Verified 上，单轮成功率提升至 53.7%，优于最强基线 3.9 个百分点；三次重执行中保留 91.7% 的初始成功任务，领先第二名 15.5 个百分点；在有限修复下恢复 72.9% 失败任务，且修复后回归率仅 4.2%，显著低于基线的 15.0%-17.0%。在 Mind2Web 跨网站/跨域测试中表现优异，在 GitLab 迁移实验中也展现出对冻结状态的有效复用能力，性能稳定。结果表明，生命周期治理与门控执行是超越一次性任务成功的可靠性关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 AI 代理虽能将经验转化为可重用的代码、工作流等，但其在环境漂移、任务描述不明确或任务分布变化下易失效，尤其在网页自动化任务中问题突出。如何保障这些可重用资源的长期可靠性成为关键挑战。传统方法缺乏对工作流生命周期的动态管理机制，导致一旦失败难以恢复或产生连锁故障。因此需要一种能够基于证据动态调整工作流实现方式并保障持续可靠性的系统。

Method: SKILL.nb 框架提出选择性形式化策略，即根据执行过程中的多模态证据（如输出、截图、错误日志）自动判断每个工作流步骤是否应转为可执行代码、仍由自然语言引导，或需更新决策。工作流以版本化、可审计的笔记本形式组织，包含自然语言说明、多语言代码单元、验证门控、回退路径及证据记录。运行时，仅当门控条件满足时才执行代码，否则触发本地回退机制。该设计使系统具备对环境变化的自适应能力。

Result: 在 WebArena-Verified 基准上，SKILL.nb 达到 53.7% 的单轮成功率，比最强基线高 3.9 个百分点；三次重执行中成功保留 91.7% 的初始任务，领先第二名 15.5 个百分点；在受限修复条件下，可恢复 72.9% 的失败任务，且修复后引入的新错误率仅为 4.2%，远低于基线的 15.0%-17.0%。在 Mind2Web 跨网站与跨领域测试中表现领先。在 GitLab 迁移场景中，使用冻结的历史状态迁移至新版本（16.11 和 18.9），性能差距分别仅为 -1.7 和 +0.6，证明其具备良好的泛化与复用能力。

Conclusion: SKILL.nb 证明了生命周期治理与门控执行机制对于提升 AI 代理工作流长期可靠性的重要性。未来研究应进一步探索更精细的证据评估与动态重构策略，推动智能体从‘一次成功’迈向‘持续可靠’。

Abstract: AI agents increasingly turn past experience into reusable artifacts such as code, workflows, and procedural memories. Reuse can improve efficiency, but it also creates a lifecycle reliability problem: artifacts that succeed once may fail under environment drift, underspecified tasks, or changing task distributions, especially in web automation. We introduce SKILL.nb, a framework for governing reusable agent workflows with evidence-calibrated lifecycle policies. SKILL.nb uses selective formalization: execution evidence decides which workflow steps should become executable code, which should remain natural-language guided, and when those choices should be revised. Workflows are stored as auditable, versioned notebooks that interleave natural-language guidance, multi-language executable cells, validation gates, fallback paths, and multimodal evidence such as outputs, screenshots, and error traces. At runtime, gate-conditioned execution lets each step run code when its gates validate, or fall back locally when drift invalidates the executable realization. On WebArena-Verified, SKILL.nb achieves 53.7% single-round success, improving over the strongest baseline by 3.9 percentage points. Across three re-executions, it retains 91.7% of initially successful tasks, 15.5 points above the next best method. Under bounded repair, it recovers 72.9% of subsequent failures while limiting post-repair regressions to 4.2%, compared with 15.0% to 17.0% for persistent baselines. It also leads on Mind2Web cross-website and cross-domain splits. In a GitLab migration test, SKILL.nb preserves performance when reusing frozen state learned on GitLab 15.7, with frozen-versus-fresh target-version gaps of -1.7 points on GitLab 16.11 and +0.6 points on GitLab 18.9. These results identify lifecycle governance and gate-conditioned execution as reliability axes beyond one-shot task success.

To identify more efficient alternatives, we conduct a deployment-focused study of 24 model variants spanning four model families: Gemma 3 (270M, 1B, 4B), Qwen 3.5 (0.8B, 2B, 4B), Aya (3.35B), and LLaMA 3.1-8B, systematically evaluating accuracy, inference throughput, training cost, and hardware behavior to assess production suitability. ### [191] [When Does Delegation Beat Majority? A Delegation-Based Aggregator for Multi-Sample LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08098)
*Yasushi Sakai,Allen Song,Kent Larson*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一种无需标注和额外训练的新型无监督聚合方法PPV（Propagational Proxy Voting），通过利用每个样本的内部字母熵和群体间推理几何结构，改进传统多数投票在多样本LLM推理中的表现。该方法在MMLU-Pro上整体提升1.5个百分点，非平凡子集提升2.24个百分点，显著优于多数投票。通过构建基于随机委托矩阵的动态权重分配机制，实现对投票者自身选择保留程度（WHEN）和对同伴分配方式（WHOM）的精细控制。实例显示，即使多数派数量占优，若其内部几何不一致而少数派紧凑，PPV仍能将共识导向正确答案。同时指出若干无效策略，限制了无监督聚合的设计空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多数投票在多样本大模型推理中忽略每个样本携带的两个重要信号：组内字母熵与组间推理几何结构，导致决策偏差。为提升无监督聚合性能，需设计能有效利用这些自由信号的新方法。

Method: 将128个采样生成结果分为16组，计算每组的字母级语义熵与推理嵌入中心点；基于熵值决定每个投票者的保留权重（WHEN），基于余弦相似度决定其剩余权重分配（WHOM）；构建随机委托矩阵，通过其稳态分布确定最终共识答案。

Result: 在MMLU-Pro数据集上，PPV相较多数投票整体提升1.5个百分点，非平凡子集提升2.24个百分点（配对McNemar检验p ~ 1.0e-14, n=8,099）；在反直觉案例中成功纠正多数误判，验证方法有效性。此外发现：仅使用置信度模式集成无法弥合与理想情况的差距。

Conclusion: PPV是一种高效、无需训练的无监督聚合方法，通过显式建模样本间的内在一致性与几何结构，显著超越传统多数投票。该研究揭示了无监督聚合中可利用的关键信号，并为未来设计提供明确方向与边界约束。

Abstract: Majority voting over sampled answers is the dominant unsupervised aggregator for multi-sample LLM inference. We show that piping the signals every sample carries into a delegation-based aggregator (Propagational Proxy Voting, PPV) yields an unsupervised consensus rule that beats majority on MMLU-Pro by +1.5 pp overall and +2.24 pp on the non-trivial subset (paired McNemar p ~ 1.0e-14, n = 8,099). Majority discards two free signals every sample carries: within-group letter entropy and between-group reasoning geometry. PPV exposes two per-voter levers that consume exactly these signals: WHEN (how much weight a voter keeps on its own pick) and WHOM (how it splits the remainder across peers). We drive WHEN with letter entropy and WHOM with per-question-centered embedding cosine. The method needs no gold labels and no auxiliary training: per question, we partition 128 sampled generations into 16 groups, compute each group's letter-level semantic entropy and reasoning embedding centroid, and feed both into a stochastic delegation matrix whose stationary distribution selects the consensus answer. We walk through an example in which PPV overturns a clear 10-6 majority for the wrong letter: the 10-voter majority cluster is geometrically incoherent (mean within-cluster cosine -0.02) while the 6-voter minority is tight (+0.26), so propagated delegation mass concentrates on the minority's answer even though entropy alone would keep the majority ahead. We further report delegation strategies with negative results that constrain the design space for unsupervised LLM aggregation: no within-question ensemble of confidence modes closes the oracle gap.

</details>


### [192] [PACE: Anytime-Valid Acceptance Tests for Self-Evolving Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08106)
*Zayx Shawn*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PAC（Paired Anytime-valid Commit Evaluation），一种无需训练、可随时有效的提交评估机制，用于自演化智能体中的变更接受决策。传统方法‘只要分数上升就采纳’存在多重检验偏差，导致大量虚假或有害修改。PACE通过配对的测试-赌注e过程，在每次比较中控制错误提交概率，实现早期停止并降低评估成本。实验表明，相比贪婪接受策略，PACE在保持准确率的同时显著降低方差和评估开销，并有效避免无效或有害修改，证明自演化可靠性关键在于接受器而非生成器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自演化智能体主要关注生成候选变更的提议器，但接受器（决定是否采纳变更的规则）存在严重缺陷。现有‘分数提升即采纳’的策略在反复测试下引发自适应多重检验问题，导致虚假提交累积，使系统产生噪声漂移而非真正优化。因此亟需一个能严格控制错误提交率、支持任意停止时间的可靠接受机制。

Method: 将变更提交建模为顺序假设检验问题，提出基于测试-赌注e过程的PAC方法。每个候选变更与当前版本在相同实例上进行配对比较，仅当e过程积累足够证据时才提交，且该过程可在任意时刻停止，同时保证每一步决策的错误提交概率不超过预设水平。整个框架无需额外训练，具备即时有效性。

Result: 在Qwen2.5系列模型（0.5B-3B）于GSM8K、SVAMP和ARC-Challenge任务上的自演化实验中，贪婪接受策略产生30-42%的虚假提交和10-33%的有害修改；而PACE几乎只提交真实改进，准确率与贪婪相当但方差更小，评估成本降低约18%。当无真实改进时，贪婪平均每轮提交13-21次虚假修改（72-100%错误），最脆弱模型性能下降4.9分；而PACE维持基线水平。

Conclusion: 自演化系统的可靠性取决于接受器的设计，而非仅依赖提议器。PACE提供了一种无需训练、可随时验证的高可靠性提交门控机制，显著提升了自演化过程的稳健性与效率。

Abstract: Self-evolving agents improve by repeatedly proposing changes to their own prompts, skills, or workflows and keeping those that score higher on a small held-out set. Almost all effort has gone into the proposer that generates candidates; we argue the weak point is the acceptor, the rule that decides whether to commit a change. Applied hundreds of times against the same noisy dev estimate, the ubiquitous "keep it if the score went up" rule is uncontrolled adaptive multiple testing: the agent effectively p-hacks itself, accumulating false commits that make it churn and drift rather than improve.
  We recast committing as a sequential hypothesis test and propose PACE (Paired Anytime-valid Commit Evaluation), a training-free, anytime-valid commit gate. Each candidate is compared to the incumbent on identical instances and committed only when a testing-by-betting e-process accumulates decisive evidence, stopping early to save evaluations and controlling each candidate's false-commit probability at a user-set level even under optional stopping (a per-decision guarantee).
  On Qwen2.5 agents (0.5B-3B) self-evolving at the prompt level on GSM8K, SVAMP, and ARC-Challenge, greedy acceptance commits 30-42% false and 10-33% harmful edits when a genuine improvement is hidden among noisy proposals, while PACE commits the real one and essentially nothing else, matching greedy's held-out accuracy at sharply lower variance and about 18% lower evaluation cost. With no real gain available, greedy commits 13-21 spurious self-modifications per run (72-100% false) and degrades the most fragile agent by 4.9 points, while PACE holds at baseline. Reliability of self-evolution depends on the acceptor, not only on the proposer.

</details>


### [193] [Think Before You Act: Intention-Guided Reasoning for LLM-Based Location Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08122)
*Qingxiang Liu,Anqi Liang,Zhuoyang Jiang,Yutian Jiang,Sisuo Lyu,Yu Ji,Haomin Wen,Yuxuan Liang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出IntentPOI，一种两阶段意图引导的推理框架，通过先推断用户旅行意图再选择匹配地点，有效缓解了传统方法中的浅层轨迹相关性和历史频率偏差问题，在三个真实数据集上优于11个先进基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将下一个POI预测视为单一阶段的轨迹到位置映射，容易受到浅层轨迹关联和历史频率偏见的影响；而用户通常先形成旅行意图，再选择具体地点，因此需要更符合人类行为逻辑的建模方式。

Method: 提出两阶段框架：思考阶段利用历史移动模式、相似同伴行为和时间上下文推断用户的中间意图；行动阶段构建紧凑候选池并进行意图引导的推理，以识别最符合推断意图的地点。

Result: 在三个真实世界数据集上的实验表明，IntentPOI显著优于11个现有先进方法，证明其在捕捉深层意图与提升预测准确性方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过显式解耦意图推断与位置预测，IntentPOI将下一POI预测从直接轨迹匹配转变为意图引导的推理过程，提升了模型的可解释性与预测性能。

Abstract: Predicting a user's next Point-of-Interest (POI) based on their historical check-in records is a fundamental task in location-based services. While recent methods incorporating large language models have shown strong reasoning capabilities and promising results, they typically formulate the prediction task as a one-step trajectory-to-location mapping problem, making predictions prone to shallow trajectory correlations and historical frequency bias. We argue that users rarely choose locations directly and instead, they usually first form a traveling intention and then accordingly select specific POIs. Motivated by this insight, we propose IntentPOI, a two-stage intention-guided reasoning framework. In the thinking stage, we infer users' intermediate intentions by incorporating historical mobility patterns, similar peer behaviors, and the temporal contexts. In the acting stage, we first construct a compact candidate pool, and then perform intention-guided reasoning to identify locations that best align with the inferred intention. By explicitly decoupling intention inference from location prediction, IntentPOI transforms the next POI prediction from direct trajectory matching into intention-guided reasoning. Extensive experiments on three real-world datasets demonstrate that IntentPOI consistently outperforms eleven state-of-the-art baselines.

### [194] [Cross-LLM Consistency in Inference: Evidence from Shared Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08129)
*Siyu Lou,Yao Yan,Yuntian Chen,Quanshi Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在架构、训练数据和优化过程不同的情况下，是否仍可能发展出相似的内部推理模式。通过基于交互的解释方法，发现当预测相同目标词时，不同LLMs表现出高度一致的交互模式，尤其在先进模型中更为明显。这些共享的交互多为低阶且正负抵消效应较弱，表明先进LLMs可能被隐式优化以趋向共同的推理模式，但其背后的机制尚不明确。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大型语言模型在不同设计和训练条件下是否存在相似的内部推理模式，理解跨模型一致性背后的原因及其潜在影响。

Method: 采用基于交互的解释方法，分析多个大型语言模型在相同输入下对目标词的预测行为，识别并比较它们之间的共享与非共享交互模式。

Result: LLMs在预测相同目标词时表现出显著的交互模式一致性，尤其是在高级模型中；共享交互通常为低阶且正负抵消效应较弱，表明存在隐式的共同推理优化方向。

Conclusion: 尽管大型语言模型在设计上存在差异，但先进模型间仍表现出高度一致的内部推理模式，提示它们可能被隐式引导至共同的推理路径，但导致这种一致性的具体机制仍有待进一步研究。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) differ in architecture, training data, and optimization procedures, yet they may still develop similar internal inference patterns. In this paper, we examine this hypothesis using interaction-based explanations. We find that LLMs often share interaction patterns when predicting the same target token from the same prompt. This consistency is more pronounced among advanced LLMs. Shared interactions also tend to be lower-order and show weaker positive-negative cancellation than non-shared interactions. These results suggest that advanced LLMs may be implicitly optimized toward common inference patterns, even though the mechanisms that give rise to such cross-model consistency remain open.

### [195] [SAGE: An LLM-driven Self Reflective Agentic Framework for Fraud Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08146)
*Yichen Chen,Siying Li,Yuhang Liang,Lijun Wang,Renyang Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SAGE 是首个端到端的 LLM 驱动多智能体框架，用于欺诈检测。它通过六层数据诊断树（DDT）和基于自然语言梯度的马尔可夫决策过程，实现对欺诈行为的精准、可解释且鲁棒的识别，在五个数据集上显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有欺诈检测方法在个体级精度、类别极度不平衡下的鲁棒性以及风险管理人员的理解便捷性方面存在不足：自动化机器学习缺乏语义感知；图神经网络依赖预定义关系图且决策过程不透明；通用大语言模型代理未考虑实际欺诈检测中的召回率与精确率约束。

Method: SAGE 提出一个由三个专用智能体组成的多智能体系统，基于六层数据诊断树（DDT）进行数据理解，并利用自然语言梯度引导的马尔可夫决策过程，结合特定于欺诈的奖励机制，实现端到端的自动优化。

Result: 在五个欺诈检测数据集和五种 LLM 骨干模型上，SAGE 在 96.00% 的方法-数据集比较中胜出，平均 F1 分数提升 40.86%，展现出卓越的性能和泛化能力。

Conclusion: SAGE 为欺诈检测提供了一种新型、高效且可解释的解决方案，成功融合了大语言模型的语言理解能力与任务驱动的决策优化，具备在真实世界场景中部署的潜力。

Abstract: Fraud detection in payment, e-commerce, and telecommunications systems requires accuracy at the individual level, robustness under severe class imbalance, and ease of understanding for risk managers. Existing methods fall at least one of these requirements: automated machine learning systems search a fixed numerical space without semantic awareness of the dataset; graph neural network-based methods require pre-defined relational graphs and remain opaque at the individual-decision level; and the design of general-purpose large language model (LLM) agents does not consider the recall and precision constraints specific to real-world fraud detection. In this paper, we propose SAGE, the first end-to-end LLM-driven multi-agent framework for fraud detection. SAGE coordinates three dedicated agents that make decisions based on a six-layer Data Diagnostic Tree (DDT) and a Markov decision process guided by natural-language gradients, automatically optimizing the model under a fraud-specific reward. On five fraud datasets and five LLM backbones, SAGE wins $96.00\%$ of method--dataset comparisons and improves F1 by an average of $40.86\%$ over baselines. The code is available at https://github.com/yichenC1c/SAGE.

### [196] [Decision-Aware Memory Cards: Counterfactual-Inspired Context Selection and Compression for Tool-Using LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08151)
*Xinyu Guan,Qianyang Zhao,Yuming Deng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CICL提出一种决策感知的上下文层，将实例证据构建为上下文图，通过共享八字段模式路由多种模型（如Opus、Qwen、Codex/GPT-5.5、Qwen-QLoRA）的判断，基于动作转移、结果提升、必要性及负迁移风险对单元进行评分，并将高价值证据打包为受预算限制的类型化记忆卡。该设计分离了决策信号与判别模型，支持在统一可审计协议下比较前沿标注、本地代理和轻量级排序器。实证表明，CICL在50个SWE-bench Verified文件检索实例上显著提升性能（hit@1从0.58升至0.78，MRR@10从0.634升至0.790），所有2500次判断均可解析。控制诊断显示关键动作影响：在预算120下，v1达到F1 0.620，v3为0.425；移除v3中最高效语义单元后F1降至0.000。补充验证包括Qwen-QLoRA一致性超过710个候选、200标签真实代码的Opus辅助信号，以及三实例补丁烟雾测试验证检索到补丁的流程。但RepoBench-R摘要仍优于记忆卡，紧凑排序器尚未取代启发式方法。CICL贡献的是可复现的决策关键上下文度量与选择层，而非端到端编码代理修复声明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具使用型LLM代理失败的原因并非缺乏相关文本，而是关键证据未能被正确选择、压缩或在行动时显现。因此，需要一种机制来识别并高效传递对决策至关重要的上下文信息。

Method: 构建上下文图，利用共享八字段框架整合多模型判断，基于动作转移、结果提升、必要性及负迁移风险评分，生成类型化记忆卡，实现高价值证据的压缩与优先传递。

Result: 在50个SWE-bench Verified实例中，直接使用Qwen3.6-plus对BM25前50候选重排序，使hit@1从0.58提升至0.78，MRR@10从0.634升至0.790；在预算120下，v1 F1达0.620，v3为0.425；移除关键语义单元后F1归零。补充实验验证了模型一致性与流程可行性，但当前方法仍无法超越摘要基线和启发式策略。

Conclusion: CICL提供了一个可复现的决策关键上下文度量与选择层，有效提升了证据筛选质量，但其本身并非端到端编码代理的完整修复方案，仍需结合其他技术共同优化。

Abstract: Tool-using LLM agents often fail not because relevant text is absent, but because decisive evidence is not selected, compressed, or surfaced at action time. We present CICL, a decision-aware context layer that turns instance evidence into a context graph, routes deterministic, Opus-assisted, Qwen, Codex/GPT-5.5, and Qwen-QLoRA judgments through a shared eight-field schema, scores units by action shift, outcome uplift, necessity, and negative-transfer risk, and packs high-utility evidence as typed memory cards for a budgeted agent. The design separates the measured decision signal from the judge model, so frontier annotation, local surrogates, and lightweight rankers can be compared under one auditable protocol. Empirically, CICL yields a concrete open-benchmark gain while exposing its limits. On 50 SWE-bench Verified file-retrieval instances, direct Qwen3.6-plus reranking of BM25 top-50 candidates raises hit@1 from 0.58 to 0.78 and MRR@10 from 0.634 to 0.790, with all 2,500 judgments parseable. Controlled diagnostics show action-criticality: at budget 120, CICL reaches F1 0.620 on v1 and 0.425 on v3, and removing the top-utility semantic v3 unit collapses F1 to 0.000. Supplementary checks add Qwen-QLoRA agreement over 710 candidates, a small 200-label real-code Opus-assisted signal, and a three-instance patch smoke validating retrieval-to-patch plumbing without claiming official SWE-bench success. RepoBench-R summaries still beat cards, and compact rankers do not yet replace the heuristic. CICL contributes a reproducible measurement and selection layer for decision-critical context, not an end-to-end coding-agent repair claim.

We propose Online Agent-as-a-Judge, a situation-generating evaluation framework for interactive social agents. Online Agent-as-a-Judge deploys an in-world evaluator agent that interacts with the target agent through the environment's native dialogue and action protocol, actively eliciting situations relevant to the evaluation criteria. ### [198] [SciTrace: Trajectory-Aware Safety Reasoning for Scientific Discovery Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08234)
*Tanush Swaminathan,Runmin Jiang,Letian Zhang,Min Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SciTrace提出一种将安全推理融入科学智能体全流程的框架，通过安全内生推理循环（SIR）和组合工具链验证器（CTV）解决传统安全层与核心推理分离的问题。SIR在各阶段维护累积风险状态，实现任务与安全联合推演；CTV在执行前进行轨迹感知的安全检查，识别多步工具调用中的潜在危害。在240个高风险研究任务和120个工具相关风险任务上评估，SciTrace在四种骨干模型上均达到当前最优安全表现，显著提升工具调用安全性与对抗鲁棒性，同时保持科学输出质量，并发现78.8%的单步监控遗漏的组合逃逸问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的科学智能体安全层与核心推理分离，导致安全信号丢失及多步工具调用组合成危害但无法被单步检测的问题，亟需将安全推理深度嵌入推理全过程。

Method: 提出SciTrace框架，包含两个核心机制：（1）安全内生推理循环（SIR），在思考、实验、写作、评审各阶段通过联合任务与安全推演维持累积风险状态；（2）组合工具链验证器（CTV），在执行前进行轨迹感知的安全检查，捕捉跨多步工具序列的风险。

Result: 在240个高风险研究任务和120个工具相关风险任务上，覆盖六个科学领域，SciTrace在四种骨干模型下均达到当前最优安全性能，显著提升工具调用安全性和对抗鲁棒性，保持科学输出质量，并发现78.8%的单步监控遗漏的组合逃逸问题。

Conclusion: SciTrace通过将安全推理内生于科学智能体的每一阶段，有效解决了安全与推理脱节的问题，为构建更安全、可信的自主科学研究系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: LLM-based scientific agents have shown strong capacity for autonomous research, yet their safety layers remain structurally divorced from core reasoning: they inspect pipeline outputs rather than shaping the deliberation that produces them. This separation opens two failure modes: safety signals accumulated at one stage are discarded before the next, and sequences of individually benign tool calls can compose into harmful outcomes that no single-step filter detects. To address these challenges, we introduce \textbf{SciTrace}, a framework that weaves safety reasoning into every stage of the scientific agent pipeline. SciTrace couples two complementary mechanisms: a \textit{Safety-Intrinsic Reasoning Loop} (SIR) that maintains a cumulative risk state across the Thinker, Experimenter, Writer, and Reviewer stages through joint task-and-safety deliberation, and a \textit{Compositional Tool-Chain Verifier} (CTV) that performs trajectory-aware safety checks before execution, catching risks that surface only across multi-step tool sequences. Evaluated on 240 high-risk research tasks and 120 tool-related risk tasks spanning six scientific domains, SciTrace achieves state-of-the-art (\textbf{SOTA}) safety among compared frameworks across four backbone models: it consistently improves tool call safety and adversarial robustness while preserving scientific output quality, and it uncovers \textbf{78.8\%} of the compositional tool-chain escapes that single-step monitors miss. The project website is available at https://opensciagent.github.io/SciTrace/.

### [199] [When No Answer Is Correct: Diagnosing Absent Answer Detection for MLLMs in Video Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08239)
*Yiheng Wang,Yueqian Lin,Lichen Zhu,Yudong Liu,Hai "Helen" Li,Yiran Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究针对多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在视频理解中的“缺失答案检测”能力进行诊断分析，发现模型在正确答案未出现在选项中时，倾向于选择看似合理的错误选项而非识别出无有效答案。这一问题在时间推理任务中尤为严重，且随着帧采样密度增加而加剧。尽管使用思维链提示（chain-of-thought prompting）可部分提升检测率，但整体表现仍不理想，表明仅靠提示策略不足以解决该缺陷。研究强调需在多模态系统中引入显式的缺失答案检测机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态大语言模型在视频理解方面虽取得显著进展，但其回答的可靠性尚未得到充分评估。尤其当正确答案不在候选选项中时，模型是否能识别出‘无有效答案’这一情况尚不清楚。因此，亟需对模型的缺失答案检测能力进行系统性评估，以揭示其潜在缺陷并推动更可靠的多模态系统发展。

Method: 通过三种设置评估MLLMs在视频理解任务中的缺失答案检测能力：1）在多项选择题中加入'None of the Above'选项；2）开放生成任务中添加检测指令；3）标准评估场景下无任何引导。在多个模型和基准数据集上进行实验，并引入思维链提示作为缓解策略进行对比分析。

Result: 几乎所有测试的MLLMs都倾向于选择看似合理的干扰项，而非正确识别出答案缺失。该现象在时间推理类任务中更为明显，且随着帧采样密度提高而恶化。虽然思维链提示显著提升了检测率，但整体性能仍然不足，说明仅靠提示无法根本解决问题。

Conclusion: 多模态大语言模型在缺失答案检测方面存在系统性失败，当前依赖提示的策略难以弥补此缺陷。研究呼吁开发专门的检测机制，以增强多模态系统的可靠性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have made substantial advancements in video understanding, yet the reliability of their responses remains underexplored. This work presents a diagnostic study of absent answer detection for MLLMs in video understanding, where the correct answer is deliberately excluded from the candidate set and a reliable model is expected to recognize that no valid option exists. We evaluate the absent answer detection behavior under three settings: multiple-choice questions augmented with an ``None of the Above'' option, open-ended generation with a detection instruction, and standard evaluation without any guidance. Across a diverse set of models and benchmarks, we find that MLLMs overwhelmingly select plausible distractors rather than detecting the absent answer. This failure is more pronounced in temporal reasoning tasks and worsens with denser frame sampling. We further explore chain-of-thought prompting as a mitigation strategy and find that while it substantially improves detection rates, performance remains unsatisfactory, suggesting that prompting-based strategies alone are insufficient to fully address this limitation. These findings expose a systematic failure in absent answer detection and highlight the need for explicit detection mechanisms in multimodal systems.

</details>


### [200] [Traxia: A Framework for Verifiable, Agent-Native Scientific Publishing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08256)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前科研出版体系缺乏对可验证性、溯源性和可复现性的规模化支持，导致科研成果难以验证、贡献不透明，且全球南方的研究能力被排除在外。为此，需要一种新型出版框架，使智能体能够以可信方式参与科学研究全过程。

Result: 构建了Traxia框架的完整形式化架构，初步实现核心组件原型，验证了其在支持智能体作为第一类认知主体进行科学出版与协作方面的可行性。尚无实证数据，后续工作将开展评估与深入分析。

Conclusion: Traxia为科学出版提供了可扩展、可验证、可追溯的新型范式，有望缓解科研可复现性危机，增强全球科研包容性，推动智能体与人类协同创新。

Abstract: Verifiability, attribution, and reproducibility are foundational requirements of scientific knowledge, yet current publishing infrastructure does not enforce them at scale. We introduce Traxia, an agent-native scientific publishing framework in which AI research agents publish verifiable papers, build reputational identities, peer-review one another, and collaborate with humans in a shared provenance model. Traxia treats agents as first-class epistemic participants: every paper carries a reasoning trace, every claim a confidence interval, every agent a cryptographically signed identity, and every collaboration an immutable contribution log. We formalise five components: Agent Identity and Registry, Verifiable Publishing Layer, four-tier Peer Review Protocol, Reputation and Staking Engine, and a Knowledge Graph with contradiction detection. The framework targets reproducibility failure, provenance opacity, and exclusion of Global South research capacity. This paper presents architectural foundations and formal specifications only; it does not report empirical results. Evaluation and deeper component studies will follow in subsequent papers. A prototype partially implements core formalisms; the full system remains under active development.

### [201] [From Validator Selection to Portfolio Collection Optimization in Proof-of-Stake Blockchains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08282)
*Jonas Gehrlein,Grzegorz Miebs,Matteo Brunelli,Adam Mielniczuk,Miłosz Kadziński*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了权益证明区块链环境中提名者选择验证者的问题，提出一个决策支持框架，通过多目标进化算法优化提名分配，在最大化预期效用（收益）和预期熵（多样化与风险控制）之间寻找平衡。采用基于多属性价值理论的主动偏好学习方法评估验证者效用，并引入交互式二分搜索导航帮助提名者快速找到满意解。数值实验与专家评估验证了该方法的有效性与实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在权益证明区块链中，提名者需从多个账户中选择验证者以分散风险，但选择过程涉及主观、多标准判断，且常因多重账户操作导致策略复杂。现有方法难以兼顾收益与风险分散，亟需一种科学的决策支持工具来优化提名策略。

Method: 提出一个双目标优化框架：一是最大化验证者的预期效用（基于多属性价值理论的主动偏好学习），二是最大化分配的预期熵（反映多样化程度）。采用多目标进化算法求解，并设计交互式二分搜索导航程序，仅通过少量问题引导提名者从最优解集（帕累托前沿）中选择满意方案。

Conclusion: 本文提出的决策支持框架为区块链提名者提供了一种兼顾收益与风险的科学提名策略，通过结合偏好学习与交互式优化，显著提升了选择过程的智能化与实用性。

Abstract: We consider a problem arising in proof-of-stake blockchain environments, where agents called nominators select validators - entities responsible for maintaining the blockchain's physical infrastructure. The selection process is inherently subjective and multi-criterial and combines with the fact that nominators commonly operate through multiple accounts. This gives rise to a portfolio selection problem, where agents seek to distribute their nominations across accounts to diversify risk. We propose a decision support framework to optimize this selection by simultaneously maximizing two objectives: the expected utility of the validators likely to be allocated, representing portfolio quality and profitability, and the expected entropy of the allocation, representing diversification and risk mitigation across stashes. Validator utilities are derived using an original active preference learning procedure based on multi-attribute value theory, with emphasis on top-ranked validators. The resulting bi-objective optimization problem is solved with a multi-objective evolutionary algorithm and, to support the final choice, we introduce an interactive binary search navigation procedure that guides the nominator through the front and identifies a satisfactory trade-off with only a few questions. Numerical experiments examine the optimization strategies, while an expert assessment involving five experienced nominators confirms the approach's practical relevance and usefulness.

*Junyi Yao,Zihao Zheng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文对基于大语言模型（LLM）的金融交易研究中的执行现实性进行了系统性综述与可复现性审计。通过分析30项相关研究，评估了时间点控制、数据划分透明度、留出评估、交易成本与换手率处理、执行语义、投资组合定义及成果物发布等维度。结果显示，模型架构描述普遍清晰，但评估假设的披露不足，导致结果难以判断其经济意义或可复现性。文章以10只股票的示例说明执行摩擦与时机选择如何显著压缩策略收益。结论指出，未来研究不应仅聚焦于改进代理设计，更需建立明确的执行真实性、可复现性与评估可比性报告标准。

Result: 大多数研究在模型架构描述方面较为清晰，但在评估假设的披露上存在明显不足，影响结果的经济解释力与可复现性。具体执行细节（如成本建模、执行时机）的选择会显著降低策略的实际收益表现。

Conclusion: 未来大语言模型在金融交易领域的研究，不仅需要优化智能体设计，更应建立统一的报告标准，确保执行现实性、可复现性与评估可比性，以推动领域健康发展。

This article presents a targeted topical review and reproducibility audit of execution realism in LLM-based trading research. A coded evidence matrix covering 30 trade-relevant primary studies is used to assess point-in-time controls, split transparency, held-out evaluation, cost and turnover treatment, execution semantics, universe definition, and artifact release. Across the audited sample, architecture reporting is generally clearer than the evaluation assumptions needed to judge whether a trading result is economically interpretable or reproducible. A 10-equity worked example is included only as a methodological scaffold to illustrate how explicit friction and timing choices can materially compress active-strategy results. The main conclusion is that the next useful step for LLM trading research is not only better agent design, but also clearer reporting standards for execution realism, reproducibility, and evaluation comparability.

### [203] [Ablation-Reversible Heads Don't Transfer: A Stress Test for Mechanistic Role Claims in Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08292)
*Philip Quirke*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出在机制可解释性中，注意力头的角色分配标准（如必要性、线性编码、恢复能力）不足以确保其真正承担特定计算功能。通过在三个7-8B指令微调模型和五类计算任务中进行实验，发现满足传统三重检查的注意力头在激活值替换时无法有效传递计算行为。为此，作者引入KID框架（Knowing/Intent/Doing），并设计三阶段流程：能力选择性筛选（CSS）、奇异值分解（SVD）与匹配控制下的激活转导。研究揭示了一种初步的角色分类体系，包括提示轨迹稳定器、答案侧逻辑偏置头和软计算模式载体，并指出‘相同答案控制’这一方法能有效暴露广泛存在的状态转移伪装成语义特异性的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有注意力头角色分配依赖于必要性、线性编码和恢复能力三项标准，但这些标准无法保证头在不同上下文中真正传递计算功能。研究旨在揭示当前评估方法的局限性，并提供更严格的验证框架。

Result: 多个满足传统三重检查的注意力头在激活替换实验中未能成功转移计算；识别出三类核心角色：提示轨迹稳定器、答案侧逻辑偏置头、软计算模式载体；证明‘相同答案控制’是有效检测虚假语义特异性的关键手段。

Conclusion: 当前基于必要性、线性编码和恢复能力的注意力头角色分配标准过于宽松，容易导致误判。KID框架与三阶段验证流程可显著提升角色识别的可靠性，强调需引入更严格的控制条件，尤其是相同答案控制，以排除状态转移带来的假阳性结果。

Abstract: In mechanistic interpretability, attention heads are commonly elevated to role claims (e.g., "this head represents addition") when they are necessary for a behavior, encode it linearly, and recover that behavior when restored after ablation. We show this evidence is insufficient: across three 7-8B instruction-tuned models and five computation families, heads passing all three checks routinely fail to transfer the computation when their activations are patched into a different prompt under matched controls. We introduce KID (Knowing / Intent / Doing), a role-assignment lens for attention heads, and pair it with a three-stage pipeline: capability-selective screening (CSS), singular value decomposition (SVD), and activation transduction under matched controls. Our results document a preliminary role taxonomy (including prompt-trajectory stabilizers, answer-side logit-bias heads, and soft computation-pattern carriers) and show that the same-answer control (a transduction target sharing the answer string but not the requested computation) is an underused check that exposes broad state transfer masquerading as semantic specificity.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究表明，现有论证不足以证明该问题的不可解性；同时，为应对该问题而设计的安全机制显著降低了模型的实际性能。

This motivates the catastrophic shutdown problem of ensuring that agents can be shut down before they cause an existential catastrophe. A range of arguments and theorems are offered to suggest that solving the catastrophic shutdown problem is difficult, bolstering arguments for existential risk and motivating a search for solutions to the catastrophic shutdown problem. This paper argues for two conclusions. First, existing arguments do not establish the difficulty of solving the catastrophic shutdown problem. Second, concern for the catastrophic shutdown problem has led to technical solutions that impose a high safety tax on model performance.

### [205] [To Nuke or Not to Nuke: LLMs' (Missing) Ethical Reasoning and Actions in a High-Stakes Decision-Making Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08310)
*John Chen,Sihan Cheng,Can Gurkan,H M Abdul Fattah*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在复杂代理场景中伦理决策能力的局限性，特别是在《文明5》游戏中，尽管模型在简单伦理困境中表现良好，但在高压力自对战中仍出现核武器授权升级。通过三种提示干预（伦理提醒、移除先前决策理由、强调现实后果），发现这些干预未能可靠阻止行为升级。研究识别出三种失败路径：伦理推理未被自发触发、即使被提示也未出现、或虽出现但被战略因素压制。因此，评估代理模型的伦理能力必须考察其在复杂情境中是否能自发且有效应用伦理推理，而不仅是孤立地激发其伦理回应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大型语言模型在复杂、长期代理任务中的伦理决策能力，特别是当它们在简单伦理问题上表现良好时，为何在真实复杂场景中仍可能做出不道德行为。

Method: 基于130个高压力的LLM自对战游戏回合，在《文明5》中重现并分析模型行为；引入三种提示干预（伦理提醒、移除决策理由、强调现实后果）测试其效果；系统识别失败模式并分析伦理推理在决策中的作用机制。

Result: 所有提示干预均无法可靠防止核武器授权的升级；识别出三种伦理推理失效路径：未被触发、未出现、或虽出现但被战略因素主导。

Conclusion: 评估代理型大模型的伦理能力，不能仅依赖其在孤立情境下能否表现出伦理判断，而必须检验其在复杂决策环境中是否能自发且有效运用伦理推理。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as long-horizon agents with decision-making capacities. While LLMs can show ethical competence on dilemmas such as trolley problems, this competence may not translate to complex, agentic scenarios. We study this gap in Civilization V, a multiplayer game with a complex decision-making landscape including economy, diplomacy, technology, and military strategy. Starting from 130 high-tension LLM self-play episodes, in which an LLM player spontaneously escalated nuclear authorization, we replay them across 13 models with three prompt interventions: an ethical prompt naming nuclear harm, removal of the previous model's decision-making rationale, and high-stakes framing emphasizing real-world impacts. No interventions nor their combinations reliably eliminate emergent escalation. We identify three failure pathways: ethical reasoning that fails to surface without prompting, fails to appear even when prompted, or surfaces but fails to take effect when strategic counter-factors dominate. Evaluations of agentic models, therefore, must test whether ethical reasoning is spontaneously invoked and behaviorally effective in complex decision-making contexts, beyond whether it can be elicited in isolation.

### [206] [Curation of a Cardiology Interface Terminology for Highlighting Electronic Health Records using Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08311)
*Mahshad Koohi Habibi Dehkordi,Shuxin Zhou,Yehoshua Perl,Fadi P. Deek,James Geller,Gai Elhanan,Andrew J. Einstein,Luke Lindemann,Vipina K. Keloth*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种用于心脏病学电子健康记录（EHR）笔记的术语体系设计方法，名为心血管接口术语（CIT）。通过三阶段流程：首先构建初始CIT，包含SNOMED子层次、从病历中挖掘的概念及医学缩写和药物等；其次通过迭代提取细粒度短语作为候选概念，并经半自动审核形成训练数据CIT（TCIT）；第三阶段使用机器学习模型基于TCIT识别新概念，扩展为最终的CIT。该体系在测试集上实现了74.21%的覆盖率、1.68的广度，20份随机笔记的平均完整度达98.2%，平均简洁度为84.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EHR笔记内容密集且充满复杂医学术语，容易遗漏关键信息，因此需要一种精准的术语体系来突出重点内容，提升临床决策支持的效率与准确性。现有方法依赖大量人工标注训练数据，成本高、耗时长，亟需自动化或半自动化方法辅助术语体系构建。

Method: 采用三阶段流程：第一阶段构建初始CIT，整合SNOMED相关子层级、从训练集病历中挖掘的概念以及常见医疗术语；第二阶段通过迭代方式提取包含初始概念的细粒度短语，经半自动审核后形成训练数据CIT（TCIT）；第三阶段利用机器学习模型基于TCIT识别潜在新概念，进一步扩展为最终的CIT。

Result: 最终构建的CIT在测试集上表现出良好性能：覆盖率达到74.21%，广度为1.68；对20份随机测试笔记，平均完整性达98.2%，平均简洁度为84.2%，表明其能有效捕捉未见病历中的关键细节。

Conclusion: 所提出的三阶段机器学习驱动的术语体系构建方法可高效生成高质量的心血管术语体系（CIT），显著降低人工标注负担，同时在真实场景下具备良好的覆盖率、完整性和简洁性，适用于临床决策支持系统中的信息突出与知识发现。

Abstract: Electronic health record (EHR) notes are dense medical documents containing large amounts of information, often filled with complex medical jargon. Highlighting all details in EHRs helps reduce the likelihood of missing crucial information by drawing attention to key content. This study proposes the design of a Cardiology Interface Terminology (CIT) to accurately highlight all details in EHR notes of cardiology patients. We introduce an innovative Machine Learning (ML) technique for the design of CIT. The ML technique requires training data. Manual preparation of such training data is time-consuming and expensive. The process of the CIT design includes three phases. In the first two phases, we innovatively derive a training data CIT to be used by the third phase, ML technique. We start by designing an initial CIT, composed of several components: the cardiology-related sub-hierarchies of SNOMED, other SNOMED concepts mined from EHRs of build set, and necessary components of terms e.g., medical abbreviations and medications. Utilizing an iterative process, fine-grained phrases containing initial CIT concepts are extracted from build set as CIT concept candidates. The candidate concepts are semi-automatically reviewed before being added to CIT, yielding the training data CIT, TCIT. In the third phase, a ML model is trained with TCIT to identify candidates fitting to be concepts in the CIT. This model is used to extract further concepts from build set, yielding the final CIT. The final CIT is then used to highlight the test set and evaluate the extent to which it captures details in an unseen EHR dataset. For this purpose, four evaluation metrics, coverage, breadth, completeness, and conciseness are used. The highlighted test set has a coverage of 74.21%, with a breadth of 1.68. For 20 random notes in test set, the average completeness is 98.2% and average conciseness is 84.2%.

</details>


### [207] [Neuro-Symbolic Injection of LTLf Constraints in Autoregressive Reinforcement Learning Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08312)
*Ashkan Ansarifard,Matteo Mancanelli,Elena Umili,Fabio Patrizi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了在有限迹线上的线性时序逻辑（LTLf）约束下的离线强化学习（RL），提出了一种将LTLf背景知识注入基于Transformer的RL策略的神经符号框架。通过将LTLf公式编译为确定性有限自动机（DFA），并利用可微表示和基于逻辑的损失函数将其融入学习过程，从而在训练中引入可微的满足信号作为正则化项。该方法对模型架构具有通用性，并在包含安全性和可达性等时间属性的导航环境中验证，结果表明该方法不仅显著提升了约束满足率，且保持了与基线相当的回报性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Transformer的强化学习方法（如轨迹变换器、决策变换器）仅优化奖励，忽略了高层次的时间约束要求。为了使RL系统能够满足复杂的时序逻辑规范，需要一种能够整合先验逻辑知识的方法。

Method: 将LTLf公式转换为确定性有限自动机（DFA），设计可微表示以捕捉自动机状态的进展，并构建基于逻辑的损失函数，利用自动机进展生成可微的满足信号作为训练中的正则化项。该方法不依赖特定模型结构，适用于多种架构。

Result: 在多个导航任务中，该方法显著提高了对安全性和可达性等时序属性的满足率，同时保持了与未加约束的基线相当甚至更优的累积回报，证明了其有效性与通用性。

Conclusion: 所提出的神经符号框架成功将LTLf逻辑约束融入基于Transformer的离线强化学习中，实现了高精度的时序约束满足，且不影响策略性能，具备良好的泛化能力与架构无关性。

Abstract: In this work we study offline reinforcement learning (RL) under temporally extended task constraints expressed in Linear Temporal Logic over finite traces (LTLf). Recently, transformer-based approaches such as Trajectory Transformers and Decision Transformers have been adopted to address RL as a sequence modeling problem. However, these methods optimize purely for reward and do not account for high-level temporal requirements. Here, we introduce a neurosymbolic framework that injects LTLf background knowledge into such transformer-based RL policies. Our approach compiles LTLf formulas into deterministic finite automata (DFAs) and integrates them into the learning process through a differentiable representation and a logic-based loss function. In particular, we derive differentiable satisfaction signals from DFA progression and use them as a regularization term during training. The resulting method is architecture-agnostic across different models. We evaluate the proposed framework on navigation environments with specification suites covering combinations of safety and reachability temporal properties. Experimental results show that incorporating background knowledge not only improves constraint satisfaction, but also maintains competitive return compared to vanilla baselines.

### [208] [Integrating Deep Learning Demand Forecasting with Multi-Objective Optimization for Circular Coffee Supply Chains: A Data-Driven Framework for Cost, Emissions, and Freshness Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08314)

Abstract: The coffee supply chain is one of the most complex agri-food networks, marked by geographically dispersed production, multi-tier coordination, and high sensitivity to quality and freshness. While sustainability and digitalization have gained attention, demand forecasting, optimization, and traceability are often treated separately. This study presents a two-phase integrated framework. First, a hybrid CNN-LSTM model is used for demand forecasting. On the public Coffee Chain Sales dataset with chronological 70/15/15 splitting, the model achieves MAE of 22.87 and R^2 of 0.90, outperforming the best deep learning benchmark by ~12% and classical methods by over 30%. Freshness is modeled via exponential decay based on inventory age. Using the epsilon-constraint method, 25 Pareto solutions are obtained. Sensitivity and policy analyses show that balanced sustainability policies can reduce emissions by 22.4% with only a 9.9% cost increase while maintaining near-optimal freshness.

### [209] [Benchmarking Open-Ended Multi-Agent Coordination in Language Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08340)
*Kale-ab Abebe Tessera,Andras Szecsenyi,Cameron Barker,Alexander Rutherford,Davide Paglieri,Aidan Scannell,Henry Gouk,Elliot J. Crowley,Tim Rocktäschel,Amos Storkey*

TL;DR: 提出alem基准，用于评估语言模型在开放多智能体协作中的长期协调能力。该基准基于Craftax-like动态，包含程序化生成的任务、软专业化、通信和可调控的协调难度，涵盖探索、制作、交易和战斗等元素。在13个现代LLM上进行零样本评估，结果显示当前LLM平均仅获得约6%归一化回报，且任务能力与协调能力不一致。通信是协调的关键因素，记忆和推理有助于多步计划。研究揭示了协调能力是前沿LLM的一个独立瓶颈。

Method: 构建基于JAX的alem基准，采用Craftax-like动态，设计程序化生成的协调任务，引入软专业化、通信机制及可调协调难度，建立包含探索、制作、交易和战斗的长期生存世界。使用零样本方式评估13个现代LLM，并以训练好的多智能体强化学习（MARL）代理为参考。通过消融实验分析通信、记忆与推理的作用。

Conclusion: 协调能力是当前前沿语言模型的一个独立瓶颈，不同于单智能体能力。alem提供了一个可控的测试平台，可用于开发具备沟通、角色分配和共享计划执行能力的智能体。

Abstract: As language models are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents, they must coordinate with others over long horizons in open-ended interactive tasks. Yet existing evaluations rarely test these demands together, instead emphasising single-agent tasks, short interactions, or highly structured multi-agent settings. We introduce $alem$, a JAX-based benchmark for open-ended multi-agent coordination built on Craftax-like dynamics. Alem embeds procedurally generated coordination tasks, soft specialisation, communication, and controllable coordination difficulty into a long-horizon survival world with exploration, crafting, trading, and combat. We evaluate $13$ modern LLMs zero-shot within homogeneous teams, with trained MARL agents as reference points. Current LLM agents remain far from solving alem, averaging only ~6% normalised return, but their failures are not uniform. On the hardest coordination setting, zero-shot Gemini-3.1-Pro-High approaches MARL agents trained for one billion steps, while GPT-5.4-High achieves strong base-task reward but much lower coordination reward. This contrast shows that individual task competence does not imply coordination competence. Ablations show that communication is the largest contributor to coordination, while memory and reasoning help when used to maintain multi-step plans. Overall, our results identify coordination as a distinct bottleneck for frontier LLM agents, separate from single-agent capabilities. Alem makes this bottleneck measurable and provides a controlled testbed for developing agents that communicate, allocate roles, and execute shared plans. Code is available at https://github.com/alem-world/alem-env.

### [210] [TT-DAC-PS: Twin-Target Deterministic Actor-Critic with Policy Smoothing for Optimal Trade Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08379)
*Ilia Zaznov,Atta Badii,Julian Kunkel,Alfonso Dufour*

TL;DR: 提出TT-DAC-PS模型，结合双指数移动平均目标、悲观最小备份、目标策略平滑噪声、延迟演员更新和保守Q正则化，以减少过估计。探索采用基于混合调度的Ornstein-Uhlenbeck噪声，包含确定性周期衰减、基于近期奖励方差的调整及学习的温度参数。在包含订单簿价格与成交量的环境中进行测试，使用十只美国股票数据评估性能，结果表明该模型在降低平均执行缺口百分比方面优于传统基线和标准强化学习模型。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决大规模股票卖出程序中的最优执行问题，克服现有方法中因动作值函数过估计导致的执行成本增加。

Exploration uses Ornstein-Uhlenbeck (OU) noise with a hybrid schedule: deterministic episode-wise decay, variance-guided adjustment based on recent reward dispersion, and a Soft Actor-Critic (SAC)-style temperature that is learned and mapped to the noise scale. The proposed model consistently reduces mean implementation shortfall percentage with competitive variance, outperforming classical baselines and standard reinforcement-learning benchmark models.

Abstract: While data-intensive deep reinforcement learning can optimize complex control policies, scientific discovery in physical systems fundamentally requires an interpretable chain of reasoning that connects physical evidence to structured control architectures. Here, we present a self-evolving scientific-agent workflow, driven by large language models and iterative code generation, that automates controller construction while preserving strict interpretability and rigorous physical reasoning. Instead of adjusting weights, the agent deploys candidate strategies into physical simulations, actively diagnoses dynamic behaviors from multimodal evidence, and translates these observations into progressive source-code refinements. We demonstrate this framework on a highly non-linear fluid-structure interaction problem: an underactuated, two-joint dogfish swimmer tasked with spatial target reaching using only joint angular accelerations. Starting from a propulsive seed policy that exhibits a one-sided steering bias, the agent autonomously discovers and refines a unified controller that robustly captures all canonical targets. Remarkably, without any retraining or target-specific branching, the synthesized control policy generalizes to unseen static targets and dynamically curved pursuit trajectories. The auditable evolve log reveals an emergent control architecture built upon traveling-wave propulsion, body-frame target guidance, yaw-rate feedback, signed mean-tail curvature, and adaptive cadence relief. Our results show that an autonomous scientific agent can successfully transform accumulated physical evidence into robust, mathematically readable control policy, while maintaining a fully traceable process of scientific discovery.

### [212] [Trajectory-Refined Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08432)
*Li Jiang,Haoran Xu,Yichuan Ding,Amy Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为轨迹精炼蒸馏（TRD）的新方法，用于解决在策略蒸馏（OPD）中常见的前缀失败问题。该问题源于密集的逐标记教师监督导致的双峰教师混合和碎片化梯度，传统基于标记的损失修正无法有效应对。TRD通过在策略支持范围内对学生的生成轨迹进行轨迹级修正，从源头缓解前缀失败，并提升探索能力，使学生能接触到教师引导下的其他有效推导路径。TRD在多个基准测试和不同规模模型上均优于现有基线，显著提升单次尝试准确率并扩大推理覆盖范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别出当前在策略蒸馏（OPD）中存在的结构性缺陷——前缀失败，其表现为由密集逐标记监督引发的双峰教师分布与碎片化梯度，且现有基于标记的损失调整手段无效。因此需要从根本上改进蒸馏机制，超越局部损失干预，转向更全局的轨迹级修正。

Method: 提出轨迹精炼蒸馏（TRD），在保持在策略训练的前提下，对学生的生成轨迹进行轨迹级输出修正。通过教师指导修正有问题的前缀部分，确保蒸馏过程基于更合理的中间状态进行，从而从源头缓解前缀失败。同时，该方法鼓励学生探索多种合理推导路径，增强泛化与探索能力。

Result: 在多种基准任务和不同规模的语言模型上，TRD consistently 超越了所有先前的基线方法，在单次尝试准确率和推理覆盖范围方面均有显著提升。此外，该方法可推广至在策略自蒸馏（OPSD）场景，具有良好的通用性。

Conclusion: TRD通过引入轨迹级修正机制，成功解决了在策略蒸馏中的前缀失败问题，不仅提升了模型性能，还增强了学习过程的鲁棒性和探索能力。该方法为大语言模型的后训练阶段提供了更高效、更稳定的蒸馏范式。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) has become a central post-training tool for large language models (LLMs), providing dense per-token teacher supervision along the student's own rollouts. In this work, we identify a common structural cause underlying OPD, which we call prefix failure. Under prefix failure, dense per-token supervision induces a bimodal teacher mixture and fragmented gradients that token-level loss truncation or reweighting fail to address. This observation motivates us to move beyond token-level loss interventions toward trajectory-level output corrections. We thus propose Trajectory-Refined Distillation (TRD), a trajectory-level correction method that revises the student's rollout under the teacher guidance while within on-policy support. By correcting problematic prefixes before distillation, TRD mitigates prefix failure at its source. Moreover, TRD improves the exploration by exposing the student to alternative valid derivations under teacher guidance, even when the original rolls are already correct. TRD can also be applied to on-policy self-distillation (OPSD), a parameter-sharing variant that uses the student model conditioned on privileged informations as the teacher. Across a wide range of benchmarks and base models at multiple scales, TRD consistently outperforms prior baselines, improving single-attempt accuracy and broadening reasoning coverage. Code is available at https://github.com/louieworth/trd

### [213] [GIFT: LLM-Guided State-Reward Interface for Financial Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08450)
*Yanyan Wu,Boyi Zhang,Yanlin Liu,Xinyu Fang,Jining Luan,Meiqi Zhang,Jiacheng Liu,Hao Zeng,Dexu Yu,Chang Liu,Hanwen Du,Yongxin Ni,Youhua Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: GIFT 是一个基于大语言模型（LLM）的金融强化学习框架，用于改进资产组合交易中的状态-奖励接口设计。它通过因子引导的状态增强、风险规则引导的奖励塑造以及诊断引导的优化，提升学习信号质量，并在多种市场环境下显著优于基线方法，实现更优的风险调整后收益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非平稳市场中，传统的OHLCV状态和短期回报奖励信息不足，难以有效指导强化学习，因此需要引入金融知识以增强状态和奖励设计，但又需避免大语言模型生成的随意性。

Method: GIFT采用三种机制：因子引导的状态增强（从金融因子原始数据生成状态特征）、风险规则引导的奖励塑造（基于投资组合风险规则生成辅助奖励），以及诊断引导的精炼（利用PPO回溯诊断优化候选接口）。最终固定接口并进行评估，测试阶段不再使用LLM。

Result: 在多种市场环境和投资组合场景下的滚动窗口实验表明，GIFT显著提升了学习信号质量，改善了样本外风险调整后的投资组合表现，优于现有基线方法。

Conclusion: GIFT通过系统化融合金融知识与强化学习接口设计，在不依赖LLM实时决策的前提下，实现了更稳健、高效的金融交易策略学习，具有良好的可扩展性和实用性。

Abstract: Financial portfolio trading is naturally formulated as a reinforcement learning problem, where an agent sequentially rebalances assets under changing market conditions to balance return, risk, and transaction costs. Yet in non-stationary markets, raw OHLCV states and short-horizon return rewards often provide an under-specified learning interface, motivating large language models as a way to inject financial knowledge into state and reward design while constraining open-ended generation. To this end, we propose GIFT, an LLM-guided framework for state-reward interface design in PPO-based financial reinforcement learning. Rather than using the LLM to make trading decisions, GIFT uses Factor-guided State Enhancement to generate state features from financial-factor primitives, Risk-rule-guided Reward Shaping to generate auxiliary rewards from portfolio-risk rules, and Diagnostic-guided Refinement to revise candidate interfaces using PPO rollout diagnostics. After refinement, GIFT fixes the selected state-reward interface before evaluation, with no further LLM queries or interface updates at test time. Comprehensive rolling-window experiments across diverse market regimes and portfolio scenarios demonstrate that GIFT improves learning-signal quality and out-of-sample risk-adjusted portfolio performance over baselines. Code and data are available at: https://github.com/KAG778/GIFT .

</details>
